# Knowledge silos are killing your team's productivity—here's how to break them down

Knowledge silos are killing your team's productivity—here's how to break them down
==================================================================================

![Nicholas Lui](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F5JyesDqDH44rQpuJxbzGbb%2Fa479c7a6f58058ac7dc1b098b70a90b6%2FNicholas_Lui.jpeg&w=48&q=75)By Nicholas Lui

Knowledge workers waste [20% of their time searching for information](https://www.mckinsey.com/industries/technology-media-and-telecommunications/our-insights/the-social-economy)
, according to McKinsey research. That's one full day every week spent hunting for documents, asking colleagues for context, and reconstructing decisions that were made just last month.

Knowledge silos—where critical information gets trapped in specific tools, teams, or individuals—create this daily frustration. The solution here isn't better communication or more documentation, but to fundamentally rethink how information flows through your organization.

Modern Enterprise Search transforms how teams access and share information. Instead of keyword hunting across dozens of apps, AI-powered enterprise search understands context and delivers answers from across your entire tech stack. This shift from document retrieval to intelligent knowledge discovery breaks down silos of knowledge that slow decision-making and stifle innovation.

The hidden cost of knowledge silos in modern work
-------------------------------------------------

The impact of silos of knowledge shows up in three painful ways that every team leader recognizes.

1.  **Decision-making bottlenecks slow everything down.**
    
    Product teams wait days for customer insights trapped in support tools while competitors ship faster. Meanwhile, marketing can't access the sales conversations that would sharpen their next campaign, and engineering rebuilds features because they never found the research explaining why the first version failed. Each missed connection compounds the damage—delays stack, duplicated work multiplies, and momentum dies across projects.
    
2.  **Productivity drains through duplicated work and constant context switching.**
    
    The average team uses multiple SaaS products and data is split between systems. This manifests as project updates existing in Slack threads, email chains, and meeting notes, and no one can find the latest version when they need it.
    
3.  **Innovation suffers when knowledge doesn't flow.**
    
    When customer success learns why features aren't adopted but product management never sees the feedback, critical insights die in silos. Sales identifies a new market segment marketing doesn't know about, so marketing keeps targeting the wrong audience. Support discovers a product improvement opportunity that never reaches engineering, so the same issue costs time again and again. Each disconnect builds on the last—what starts as a missed conversation becomes a pattern of lost opportunities that compounds into genuine competitive disadvantage.
    

Organizations with effective knowledge management are better able to focus on the work that matters, focusing on outcomes and not busywork.

Why traditional approaches to breaking silos fail
-------------------------------------------------

Most organizations try to solve knowledge silos with more meetings, better documentation, or adding collaboration tools. These work to an extent, but leave much to be desired.

Manual documentation fails because it requires someone to predict what information will be valuable later and then maintain it perfectly. Real knowledge lives in conversations, decisions, and iterations that happen too fast for traditional documentation to capture.

Communications tools preserve context, but it means there is yet another source of data to track down, correlate, and piece together. Adding another tool just creates another place to search.

This is where enterprise search fundamentally differs from traditional approaches. Rather than adding complexity, modern enterprise search solutions connect existing tools while maintaining their individual strengths.

The modern solution: Enterprise search that actually works
----------------------------------------------------------

Enterprise search represents a paradigm shift from finding documents to finding answers. Unlike traditional search that relies on keyword matching, AI-powered enterprise search understands context and intent across your entire knowledge ecosystem.

Modern enterprise search solutions like [Notion's Enterprise Search](https://www.notion.com/product/enterprise-search)
 connect your entire tech stack—Slack, GitHub, Google Drive, Salesforce—without creating another layer of complexity. Instead of searching each tool separately for exact keywords, you ask questions in natural language and get synthesized answers that pull from everywhere.

Consider asking "What did we decide about pricing in Q3?". While traditional search would return dozens of documents to sift through, Enterprise Search with AI delivers a synthesized answer that references the Slack discussion, the meeting notes in your workspace, and the final decision in your project management tool. No more reading through 50 documents to reconstruct a decision.

Compared with many traditional enterprise search tools, Notion pairs AI-driven understanding with a connected workspace, so teams can search and act in the same place. Instead of switching between a separate search interface and your docs or projects, results open directly where work already lives.

Since it’s integrated, Notion’s AI-powered Enterprise Search automatically respects permissions while making everything discoverable to those who need it. Your sales team can't see engineering's internal discussions, but they can find the product roadmap updates that affect their deals. Customer success can access relevant support tickets without seeing sensitive customer data they shouldn't have.

This approach differs significantly from traditional enterprise search vendors that require complex implementation and separate interfaces. Modern solutions embed search directly into existing workflows, making knowledge discovery natural rather than disruptive.

Building an integrated workspace that breaks down silos
-------------------------------------------------------

Connected search solves immediate problems, but true transformation comes from moving beyond integration to consolidation. Having everything in one workspace eliminates the friction that maintains silos of knowledge.

The distinction between integration and consolidation matters. Integration connects separate tools through APIs and workflows. Consolidation brings work into a unified environment where knowledge flows naturally. While integration helps, consolidation transforms how teams actually work.

Consider how workflows change when everything connects in a single workspace. Meeting notes automatically become project updates. Customer feedback flows directly into product roadmaps. GitHub issues live alongside design files. Code reviews reference customer requests. Support tickets inform product decisions.

This integration creates natural knowledge flow. When a customer success manager logs feedback in the same workspace where product managers plan features, that feedback gets seen and acted on. When sales conversations happen in the same space as marketing content creation, messaging stays aligned with customer reality.

[dbt Labs experienced this transformation firsthand](https://www.notion.com/blog/how-were-killing-software-sprawl-by-using-our-own-product)
. After consolidating their workspace, they achieved a 73% increase in knowledge base engagement. Teams started contributing to and using shared knowledge because it was easy to find and update.

The key difference from traditional enterprise knowledge management platforms is starting with workflows, not tools. Map how information currently moves through your organization, identify the biggest bottlenecks, then build connections that eliminate friction.

Overcoming implementation challenges with enterprise search
-----------------------------------------------------------

Large organizations face specific technical and organizational challenges when implementing enterprise search solutions. Understanding these challenges and how modern platforms address them is crucial for successful adoption.

**Data migration and legacy system integration** represent the biggest technical hurdles. Many enterprise search implementations fail because they can't effectively connect with existing systems. Modern solutions like Notion address this through pre-built connectors and APIs that work with common enterprise tools without requiring extensive custom development.

**Change management at scale** requires careful planning. Teams comfortable with current workflows resist new systems, even when they solve real problems. Start with pilot programs that demonstrate clear value before rolling out organization-wide. Focus on teams experiencing the most pain from knowledge silos—they become advocates for broader adoption.

**Performance and scalability** matter as organizations grow. Enterprise search must handle increasing data volumes and user loads without degrading performance. Modern cloud-native solutions scale automatically, but verify performance benchmarks for organizations of your size.

Getting started: Your roadmap to connected knowledge
----------------------------------------------------

Breaking down knowledge silos requires a practical, phased approach that demonstrates value quickly while building toward comprehensive transformation.

**Start with an audit.** Map where knowledge currently lives and identify the most painful silos. Which teams repeatedly ask for the same information? Where do decisions get delayed waiting for context? What knowledge gets recreated because teams can't find the original? Document specific examples and time costs to build your business case.

**Prioritize high-impact connections.** Focus on connecting the tools that create the biggest bottlenecks first. If sales and marketing use different systems but need to share customer insights constantly, start there. If engineering and product management struggle to coordinate on roadmap decisions, make that connection your priority.

**Begin small and demonstrate value.** Pick one team or project to pilot your enterprise search approach. Show how connected knowledge reduces their time spent hunting for information. Document the time savings and improved decision speed. Use these wins to build support for broader implementation.

**Address change management proactively.** Teams comfortable with their current silos need to see clear benefits before they'll change. Start with the teams that feel the most pain from disconnected knowledge. Let early adopters become advocates who help other teams see the value of breaking down information silos.

**Measure what matters.** Track time spent searching, decision speed, and knowledge reuse. These metrics help you optimize your approach and demonstrate ROI to stakeholders who control budgets. Organizations typically see 20-30% time savings on information retrieval within the first quarter of implementation.

The goal isn't to eliminate all tools immediately. It's to create intelligent connections that let knowledge flow naturally to where it's needed, transforming silos of knowledge into connected, searchable resources.

Ready to break down your knowledge silos? [Explore Notion's AI-powered knowledge management](https://www.notion.com/product/knowledge-management)
 to see how enterprise search transforms your team's productivity. Experience how connected knowledge changes everything with a free trial that demonstrates real-world value in your existing workflows.

[Try Notion for free](https://www.notion.com/signup)
, or [check out what a successful implementation feels like](https://demo.hellonotion.com/psl/enterprise-search)
.

### FAQs

What exactly are knowledge silos and how do I know if my team has them?

Knowledge silos occur when information is trapped in specific tools, teams, or individuals. Signs include repeated requests for the same information, decisions delayed waiting for data, and teams unknowingly duplicating work because they can't see what others are doing. If your team spends significant time asking "Where did we document that decision?" or "Who has the latest version?", you're experiencing knowledge silos.

How is enterprise search different from the search bar in my current tools?

Enterprise search uses AI to understand context and intent across all your tools simultaneously. Instead of searching each app separately for exact keywords, you ask questions in natural language and get synthesized answers that pull from everywhere—respecting permissions while breaking down barriers. Traditional search finds documents; enterprise search finds answers.

How do we handle change management when implementing enterprise search across large teams?

Start with pilot programs focusing on teams experiencing the most pain from knowledge silos. Document specific time savings and productivity improvements to build advocacy. Provide clear training on new workflows and celebrate early wins. Most resistance comes from uncertainty about benefits—concrete examples from peer teams overcome this effectively.

¿Con qué proveedores de calendario es compatible Notion Calendar?

Ahora mismo, Notion Calendar está integrado y sincronizado con las cuentas de Google Calendar y con calendarios de Apple iCloud. Pronto añadiremos compatibilidad con otros proveedores como Outlook.

¿Notion Calendar está disponible para dispositivos móviles?

Sí, Notion Calendar está disponible para iPhone y Android. Sabemos que algunos usuarios quieren una versión optimizada para tablets, como el iPad, y estamos trabajando para ofrecer la mejor experiencia en todas las plataformas.

¿Notion Calendar hace que Google Calendar esté sincronizado con Notion?

Notion Calendar permite ver los elementos de tu base de datos de Notion junto con los eventos de tu calendario de Google. De esta manera, podrás visualizar cronogramas de proyectos y plazos de tareas de una forma simplificada junto a otro tipo de eventos programados. Aunque todavía no es posible importar eventos de Google Calendar directamente a una base de datos, siempre estamos buscando nuevas formas de que Notion confluya e interactúe con los calendarios. ¡Ojo a nuestras próximas novedades!

### Meet Notion

Write, plan, organize. In one AI-powered workspace.

Questions & answers
-------------------

What's included with Notion?

We recommend our Business or Enterprise plans for companies. Both include the full Notion platform—docs, databases, integrations, API/MCP, and enterprise-grade security—plus all AI capabilities: Meeting Notes, Enterprise Search, Deep Research, AI Writer, and Agents. All in one connected AI-powered workspace.

Does Notion have Enterprise-grade security?

Yes. Learn more at [notion.com/security](https://www.notion.com/security?_gl=1*1d252so*_gcl_au*MTE4MTUwOTUwMy4xNzY5Mzg3MTY4*_ga*MTc3OTQxNjE1MS4xNzY5Mzg3MTY4*_ga_9ZJ8CB186L*czE3NjkzODcxNjckbzEkZzEkdDE3NjkzODgxMTYkajYwJGwwJGgw)
 or [notion.com/help/notion-ai-security-practices](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-ai-security-practices?_gl=1*1d252so*_gcl_au*MTE4MTUwOTUwMy4xNzY5Mzg3MTY4*_ga*MTc3OTQxNjE1MS4xNzY5Mzg3MTY4*_ga_9ZJ8CB186L*czE3NjkzODcxNjckbzEkZzEkdDE3NjkzODgxMTYkajYwJGwwJGgw)
. For specific requirements, [your Sales Representative](https://info.notion.so/switch-new/notion-vs-confluence#cn-form-id)
 can provide access to our Security Portal under NDA.

How can I migrate to Notion?

[Notion's Confluence Importer](https://www.notion.com/help/import-from-confluence?_gl=1*plamts*_gcl_au*MTE4MTUwOTUwMy4xNzY5Mzg3MTY4*_ga*MTc3OTQxNjE1MS4xNzY5Mzg3MTY4*_ga_9ZJ8CB186L*czE3NjkzOTk5NDkkbzIkZzEkdDE3NjkzOTk5NzIkajM3JGwwJGgw)
 makes it easy to bring your work over—whether you're moving a few projects or your entire workspace. For larger migrations, we recommend [connecting with your Sales Representative](https://info.notion.so/switch-new/notion-vs-confluence#cn-form-id)
 to go through our Migration Assessment. This helps us understand your needs and figure out the best way to support your transition.

Does Notion integrate with JIRA?

Yes! Notion integrates with JIRA in multiple ways — from seamless search and link previews to full database syncing with real-time updates. Our new 2-way sync even lets you edit work items (Owner, Status, Priority) and add comments directly in Notion, with changes automatically reflected in JIRA.

I'm currently using Confluence on-prem and need to migrate, how can Notion help?

Atlassian's Data Center sunset means you'll migrate either way. With Notion you can consolidate docs, projects, and AI into one connected workspace people actually adopt. [Schedule time with our Sales team](https://info.notion.so/switch-new/notion-vs-confluence#cn-form-id)
 to review your requirements and see how we can support your migration.

Create your own

### Custom Agents

Each Custom Agent gets its own permissions, just like a teammate. You decide what it can read and write across Notion, Slack, Mail, Calendar, and MCP integrations.

### Notion Agent

Inherits your permissions, so it can see what you see. It can search across your workspace and connected tools to take action in Notion.

Built for enterprise confidence
-------------------------------

Notion Agents are built to be safe and transparent by design. Every agent run is logged, and all changes are reversible.

### Admin controls and analytics

Workspace admins can monitor Custom Agent usage and Notion credit consumption. Every agent run is logged with full audit trails showing what triggered it, what it did, and why.

![Admin control panel](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F65h4wy89LvYgq3c4KsQ9qG%2F12aa7b621011be3369a83e08b46082d1%2Fimage.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Configurable permissions

Notion Agent inherits your permissions. Custom Agents offer page-level access control.

### Reversible changes

Built on Notion's collaboration layer. Undo any change with version history.

### Your data stays private

Notion doesn't train AI models on your content. Enterprise customers get zero data retention.

Questions & answers
-------------------

What are Custom Agents?

Custom Agents automate recurring work for your entire team. One person sets up a workflow: what data to pull, how to format it, where to post it. Set a trigger or schedule, and the agent handles it from there—24/7, whether you're online or not. One person builds it, and the whole team benefits. [Learn more.](https://www.notion.com/help/custom-agent)

What's the difference between Custom Agents and Notion Agent?

[Custom Agents](https://www.notion.com/help/custom-agent)
 are team-wide AI teammates that run automatically on schedules or triggers. [Notion Agent](https://www.notion.com/help/personal-agent)
 is a personal AI assistant that works on-demand when you ask. All Notion users get Notion Agent. Business and Enterprise customers get Custom Agents, priced under the Notion credit system.

Who can create Custom Agents?

Anyone on a Business or Enterprise plan, including Business trials, can create Custom Agents by default. Business and enterprise admins can limit who can create them from the admin dashboard.

What tools and integrations are compatible with Custom Agents?

**Slack:** Read and post messages in public channels. Trigger agents from emoji reactions and mentions. Private channels coming soon.

**Mail**: Read, organize, and draft emails automatically. Agents can apply labels, sync emails to Notion databases, and run on triggers like new emails from specific senders. [Learn more.](https://www.notion.com/help/guides/manage-your-inbox-and-calendar-with-custom-agents)

**Calendar**: View your schedule, find meeting times, and create or update events. Agents can prep you for meetings, coordinate availability across participants, and run on triggers like event created, updated, or cancelled. [Learn more.](https://www.notion.com/help/guides/manage-your-inbox-and-calendar-with-custom-agents)

**Notion MCP**: Connect to external apps via the Model Context Protocol. Use pre-configured partner integrations, including Linear, Figma, HubSpot, Ramp, Wiz, Stripe, GitHub, Intercom, Amplitude, Attio, and Sentry. Or connect too any custom MCP server (including internal tooling) with the Custom MCP connection. [Learn more.](https://www.notion.com/help/guides/connect-custom-agents-to-mcp-integrations)

What can admins control with Custom Agents?

Business and Enterprise admins have visibility and control over how Custom Agents are used across their workspace. You control who can create agents, what each agent can access, and can disable them at any time. Every run is logged, so changes are visible and reversible.

**Manage who can create agents.** Set creation permissions in Settings → Notion AI.

**Disable agents anytime.** Stop all runs, edits, and chats for any agent.

**View all workspace agents and their access.** See every agent, what it can access, and who created it.

**Track Notion credit usage.** Monitor real-time usage, see which agents consume the most credits, and get notified at 80% and 100%.

Is my data secure with Custom Agents?

Yes. Agents follow your permissions, every run is logged, and all changes are reversible. Notion doesn't train AI models on your content, and Enterprise customers get zero data retention.

How much do Custom Agents cost?

Starting May 4, 2026, Custom Agents will run on Notion credits, available as an add-on to Business and Enterprise plans. The more work they do for you, the more credits they use.

Monthly Notion credits are $10 per 1,000 credits. Buy what you need, from a few hundred to thousands. They’re shared across your workspace and reset monthly.

If you have an account team, they can help you right-size credits at higher volumes with flexible options like annual and on-demand credits.

How do Notion credits work?

Notion credits are used to run Custom Agents and are available as an add-on for Business and Enterprise plans. How many credits a Custom Agent uses depends on the task. Simple tasks use fewer credits, while more complex, multi-step workflows use more. [Learn more.](https://www.notion.com/help/custom-agent-pricing)

Monthly Notion credits are shared across the workspace and reset every month. Unused credits don't roll over. Additional credit options are available through our sales team.

All other AI features—Notion Agent, AI Meeting Notes, Enterprise Search—are included in Business and Enterprise plans at no additional cost.

Questions & Answers
-------------------

How do I start using AI Meeting Notes in Notion?

To start, type `/meet` on any Notion page, join a meeting from your Notion Calendar, or Notion will send a gentle reminder when it automatically detects meetings. AI Meeting Notes will begin capturing your meeting and generate an organized summary as soon as the meeting’s over.

Does AI Meeting Notes work with Zoom, Google Meet, and Microsoft Teams?

Yes! AI Meeting Notes in Notion records system audio, so you can capture Zoom meetings, Google Meet calls, and Teams meeting—no bots or extra software required.

Can AI Meeting Notes create action items automatically?

Absolutely. Notion's AI analyzes your meeting transcript to generate summaries and action items, saving your team hours of manual work.

How fast are the summaries available after a meeting?

AI Meeting Notes generates summaries instantly after the meeting ends—no waiting. Your team can put action items to work right away.

Can I search across past meeting notes?

Yes! Every transcript, summary, decision, and action item is saved in Notion and fully searchable across your workspace using Notion AI.

Is my meeting data secure?

Yes. You control exactly who can see your meeting notes and transcripts. Plus, Notion provides built-in privacy settings and one-click consent collection before meetings start.

Why use Notion’s AI Meeting Notes instead of other meeting note apps?

Unlike standalone apps, AI Meeting Notes lives directly in your Notion workspace—meaning your notes, tasks, and projects stay seamlessly connected. No switching tools, no lost context.

What languages does AI Meeting Notes support?

AI Meeting Notes supports 16 languages including English, French, Japanese and more.

Can I use AI Meeting Notes for any type of meeting?

Yes, you can use AI Meeting Notes for any meeting! Whether it's a 1:1s, team sync, sales calls, AI will create a helpful summary based on the context to fit your needs.

What should I look out for when buying meeting notes products?

It’s a complicated market–check out our handy [buyer’s guide](https://www.notion.com/product/ai-meeting-notes/ai-meeting-software-buyers-guide)
 for a breakdown on what to look out for.

# What it actually takes to make enterprise search work in your organization

What it actually takes to make enterprise search work in your organization
==========================================================================

![Nicholas Lui](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F5JyesDqDH44rQpuJxbzGbb%2Fa479c7a6f58058ac7dc1b098b70a90b6%2FNicholas_Lui.jpeg&w=48&q=75)By Nicholas Lui

### What it actually takes to make enterprise search work in your organization

[Enterprise search](https://www.notion.com/product/enterprise-search)
 rollouts fail when the system works, but behavior never changes.

Teams connect a few sources, announce a launch, and expect adoption to follow. Months later, people still ask the same questions in chat, reuse stale docs, and recreate work.

Plan for two tracks from day one:

*   **Technology:**
    
    connectors, indexing, relevance tuning, and permission enforcement.
    
*   **Operations:**
    
    scope, ownership, onboarding, and governance.
    

### Set expectations early

A rollout has three milestones:

1.  **Launch:**
    
    people can access search, and permissions are correct.
    
2.  **Usefulness:**
    
    common questions return current, clear results.
    
3.  **Adoption:**
    
    search becomes the default way to find answers.
    

If leadership expects immediate value, define what “good” looks like in week one and month one. Make the timeline about trust, not completion.

### Step 1: Audit your information architecture before you connect everything

Search will surface what already exists, including duplicates and outdated “final” files.

Start by mapping where knowledge lives and who owns it. Document what each source contains, who maintains it, and the failure modes you already see—duplicates, unclear titles, stale content. Then, fix the high-impact gaps before they become top results.

### Step 2: Connect the surfaces that matter most

Notion's strength is pulling context from everywhere—docs, communications, work tracking—[all in one search result](https://www.notion.com/help/guides/connected-workspace-for-product-teams-to-collaborate-ideate-and-launch)
.

Don't start by limiting. Start by connecting the three surfaces your teams depend on:

1.  A primary docs surface.
    
2.  A communication surface where context and links show up.
    
3.  A system that tracks work status.
    

When these are wired together, search becomes intelligence, enabling faster iteration cycles.

### Step 3: Prove permissions with tests

Permission leaks destroy trust.

Test with real role-based accounts and edge cases like private channels, link-shared files, and group shares. Confirm that the same query returns different results for different roles.

### Step 4: Set governance before the first broad announcement

Define the operating model:

*   Who can add sources.
    
*   Who owns relevance feedback.
    
*   Who archives duplicates and marks a source of truth.
    

Search quality is a content ownership problem as much as a technical one.

### Step 5: Pilot with the right people

A pilot should include:

*   Power users who know the current system.
    
*   Newer teammates who do not.
    
*   One or two high-stakes teams where wrong answers have real consequences.
    

Measure success with a simple question: “Can people answer common questions without a follow-up ping?”

### Step 6: Treat onboarding as product work

Most people will not “discover” search.

Ship a short quick start with example queries. Provide one place to report quality issues. Repeat the basics after launch, when usage typically drops.

### Step 7: Operate search like a system

Search quality drifts when content owners change, titles drift, and duplicates accumulate.

Set a recurring review of top queries and low-satisfaction queries. Fix the issues that block trust.

### The practical takeaway

Enterprise search is an internal product rollout.

When ownership and governance are clear, the technology has a chance to matter. [Visualize having information at your fingertips](https://demo.hellonotion.com/psl/enterprise-search)
.

### About Nicholas Lui

Software Engineer at Notion

Community

Create a support bot that monitors our support Slack channel, searches the Help Center, and responds in threads with brief, cited answers while logging all questions and answers to a “Questions & Answers” Database. When answers aren't found, create a task in a “Knowledge Base Update Requests Database” with the suggested content and Slack thread links. Use the 👍/👎 feedback reactions in Slack to update the status of the “Question & Answer” accordingly to “Resolved” or “Unresolved.”

[Resolve support tickets in Slack](https://www.notion.com/product/ai/use-cases/resolve-support-tickets-in-slack)

![](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F4Y3s0uwG5XEPb8ok2ItRB3%2F543df3d99f04f1154990fee23f8de1c6%2Fscruff_thumb_for_ai_Page.png&w=3840&q=75)

[Respond to security alerts faster](https://www.notion.com/product/ai/use-cases/respond-to-security-alerts-faster)

Route product feedback from Slack to the correct engineering team, automatically. This Custom Agent monitors a Slack channel for bugs and feature requests, cross-posts to the relevant team's channel, and files new tickets. It uses a routing rules page as its memory, starting blank and updating itself based on input over time.

[Triage product feedback](https://www.notion.com/product/ai/use-cases/triage-product-feedback)

![](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F4rBL7XBXwCKjDejV31WCOd%2F82e2f6ec294eba050334a1a3b57a6163%2FCustomer_Story_Scout_Thumb.png&w=3840&q=75)

[Find your next customer story](https://www.notion.com/product/ai/use-cases/find-your-next-customer-story)

Build a Custom Agent that identifies and summarizes the latest updates from a project tracking database. The update should include a summary of what was completed, what's planned, and a table of all active projects. Every week, the agent should create a new update, populate it with the latest project statuses, and tag team members to review and edit their respective sections.

[Automate weekly reporting](https://www.notion.com/product/ai/use-cases/automate-weekly-reporting)

### Mobile App

![Mobile App](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=%2Ffront-static%2Fpages%2Fcalendar%2Fnotion-calendar-mobile-v3.png&w=1080&q=75)

[Apple App Store](https://apps.apple.com/app/notion-calendar/id1607562761)
[Google Play](https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.cron.calendar&referrer=referer%3D)

Which calendar provider(s) is Notion Calendar compatible with?

Currently, Notion Calendar integrates and syncs with Google Calendar accounts, Outlook Calendars, and Apple iCloud-synced Calendars.

Is Notion Calendar available on mobile devices?

Yes, Notion Calendar is available for iPhone and Android devices. We know some users are looking for an optimized version for tablet devices, such as iPad, and are working to make Notion Calendar the best experience on all platforms.

Does Notion Calendar bring Google Calendar sync to Notion?

Notion Calendar allows you to view your Notion database items alongside your Google Calendar events. This offers a streamlined way to see project timelines and task due dates alongside other scheduled events. However, importing Google Calendar events directly into a Notion database is not yet possible. We’re always exploring new ways for Notion and calendars to interact. Expect exciting developments soon!

# Careers at Notion | We're Hiring!

Play

Uh-oh! It looks like your ad blocker is preventing the video from playing.

![](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=%2Ffront-static%2Fillustrated-icons%2FcatLookingUp.png&w=384&q=75)

Our values
----------

![](https://www.notion.com/front-static/illustrated-icons/people1.png)

Customer in every room

This value is at the heart of our mission: we are a tool company, and we exist to help our customers do their life’s work. Serving customers is our only quest. Anything else is secondary. This is especially true in a fast-changing time like today: we cannot go wrong by making our customers successful.

![](https://www.notion.com/front-static/illustrated-icons/target.png)

Own the outcome

AI commoditized a lot of capabilities. What really matters is agency: the ability to spot opportunities, take initiative, and own the outcome. Notion was built by people no more extraordinary than you, so we don’t wait for someone else to define the path. Agency is a muscle. Exercise it!

![](https://www.notion.com/front-static/illustrated-icons/chartLine.png)

Why not today

The AI era is extremely competitive. In this environment, collective urgency and speed are the best thing to help a company survive and thrive. Instead of saying “let’s do it next week,” we make a habit of asking “why not today?”

![](https://www.notion.com/front-static/illustrated-icons/flower.png)

Direct and kind

Notion is a kind group of humans. We believe dialing up our collective directness in this moment will accelerate how we build trust, win more, and drive better outcomes for our customers. This, in turn, makes the work a lot more fun and fulfilling.

Life at Notion
--------------

Notion is an in-person company. We come together three days a week: Monday, Tuesday, and Thursday — because the best collaboration tends to sneak up on you. A quick question becomes a whiteboard session. A lunch reshapes a plan. Togetherness is what gives it meaning.

Benefits
--------

Health insurance

Medical, dental, and vision insurance for you and your dependents, with premiums covered in most cases.

Time off

Flexible paid vacation, holidays, and a company-wide year end closure.

Mental health

Therapy, coaching, medication management, and EAP services, for you and your dependents.

Parental leave

Paid parental leave for biological, adoptive and foster parents.

Family forming & fertility

Carrot funds for family-forming services and fertility treatments, whatever your path to parenthood looks like.

Lifestyle

A monthly stipend to spend on what matters to you: dining, hobbies, fitness, and more. Gender affirmation funds are also available outside of the monthly stipend.

Retirement

Retirement and pension plans with a company match.

Commuter

Funds towards your commute to the office.

Learning & development

Funds for courses, training and subscriptions to keep growing in your role.

And more…

A Notion x Art Pass to visit museums around the world. A phone stipend. And of course, lunch and snacks in the office.

Los agentes personalizados automatizan el trabajo repetitivo de todo tu equipo
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Las respuestas, tareas y actualizaciones se gestionan solas, incluso mientras duermes. Solo tienes que configurarlo todo una vez y los flujos de trabajo funcionarán por su cuenta.

![custom-agent-hero-static](https://images.ctfassets.net/spoqsaf9291f/PxonT2OYW98z2zblXpzQV/54201835140efd39fd8c038218e705d6/custom-agents-16-9.gif)

Agentes de preguntasRespuestas al instante para las preguntas de siempre
------------------------------------------------------------------------

Responde a preguntas utilizando la información de Notion y las herramientas conectadas.

![](https://images.ctfassets.net/spoqsaf9291f/2B3Njy6gE23eBF6wbQGjYX/6625dbfc6abdaa0cf185e4ff178f79cd/QA_Agent_Modal_Light_1x1_1x.gif)

Agentes de gestión de tareasDistribuye automáticamente el trabajo que recibes
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Registra automáticamente las tareas entrantes para clasificarlas y enviarlas al equipo correspondiente.

![](https://images.ctfassets.net/spoqsaf9291f/6sFefiN0JTyO0qOVBhqVNx/a2063c371035f73e79cb376ada7ceb37/Task_Agent_Modal_Light_1x1_1x.gif)

Agentes de informes de proyectosRecibe informes cuando a ti te interese
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

Recopila y resume las últimas novedades para redactar informes recurrentes.

![](https://images.ctfassets.net/spoqsaf9291f/7in6AoRX2HJdgeDNZJDUTD/228a6685ca5a2857ac8992844a265e63/Status_Reporter_Light_1x1_1x.gif)

### Personal y privado, solo para ti

Aprende tu estilo, sigue tus instrucciones y se adapta a tu forma de trabajar.

![Wiki de la empresa Acme S. A.](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2Famc36MOo8lkpoCaFq8Nsj%2Fff4306cd6b72e6f04429b6a017fe8fa9%2Fimage.png&w=3840&q=75)

> Nuestro equipo está dejando por completo la gestión manual del trabajo en bases de datos de Notion y está pasando a hacerlo todo hablando con los agentes de Notion.

![Acme](https://images.ctfassets.net/spoqsaf9291f/3BUzpMbL7NbobzqujIFvV4/7e40b5f7377818f4f1617b3ad88c5b66/Every_logo_black.svg)

**Brandon Gell**Director de operaciones, Every

Funciona en las herramientas que tu equipo ya utiliza
-----------------------------------------------------

Los agentes de Notion utilizan tus documentos y bases de datos como contexto. Funcionan dentro de Notion y se integran con Slack, Notion Mail, Calendar y otras herramientas. Se acabó rehacer la información e ir saltando de una app a otra.

![Conexiones de IA](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F6etORkkgs3AdQnQHS1kWEu%2F1c5fc8d6be84d8f6ba3e551f964d7bf1%2Fimage.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Agentes personalizados

Cada agente personalizado tiene sus propios permisos, como si fuera un miembro más del equipo. Tú decides lo que puede consultar y modificar en Notion, Slack, Notion Mail, Calendar y las integraciones MCP.

### Agente de Notion

El agente hereda tus permisos, así que puede ver lo mismo que tú. Puede buscar en tu espacio de trabajo y en las herramientas conectadas para actuar dentro de Notion.

Diseñado para ofrecer garantías a nivel empresarial
---------------------------------------------------

Los agentes de Notion están diseñados desde el principio para ser seguros y transparentes. Cada ejecución queda registrada y todos los cambios se pueden deshacer.

### Controles y estadísticas para administradores

Los administradores del espacio de trabajo pueden supervisar el uso de los agentes personalizados y el consumo de créditos de Notion. Cada ejecución queda registrada con un historial completo que muestra qué la ha activado, qué hizo y por qué.

![Panel de control de administrador](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F65h4wy89LvYgq3c4KsQ9qG%2F12aa7b621011be3369a83e08b46082d1%2Fimage.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Permisos personalizables

El agente de Notion hereda tus permisos, mientras que los agentes personalizados permiten controlar el acceso de cada página.

### Cambios reversibles

Una función integrada en la capa de colaboración de Notion. Puedes deshacer cualquier cambio desde el historial de versiones.

### Tus datos siempre serán privados

Notion no usa tu contenido para entrenar sus modelos de IA. Además, en los planes Enterprise no se conservan los datos.

Seguridad de nivel empresarial con control total
------------------------------------------------

![Insignias de seguridad](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F7IQzSUuUqqBkTtWPkQtAVf%2Fa5738db09e9959211390eb61f31e2903%2Fimage.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Desarrollado para cumplir la normativa

Aplicamos prácticas de desarrollo seguras, avaladas por certificaciones SOC 2 e ISO, que incluyen modelado de amenazas, revisiones de seguridad y pruebas continuas.

### Protección frente a inyecciones de indicaciones

Detección avanzada de comandos ocultos en archivos subidos, aviso de enlaces sospechosos para su validación y control del contenido externo por parte de los administradores.

[Más información →→](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/how-notion-protects-against-prompt-injection-risks)

### Control de acceso granular

Los creadores pueden configurar con precisión qué puede ver y hacer cada agente personalizado, página por página y en cada app.

### Controles de administración del plan Enterprise para la creación de agentes

Los administradores del espacio de trabajo gestionan quién puede crear agentes personalizados y conectarlos a herramientas externas, como servidores MCP.

Preguntas y respuestas
----------------------

¿Qué son los agentes personalizados?

Los agentes personalizados automatizan el trabajo repetitivo de todo el equipo. Una persona configura el flujo de trabajo: qué datos recopilar, cómo darles formato y dónde publicarlos. Basta con definir un disparador o una programación y el agente se encarga del resto, las 24 horas del día, estés conectado o no. Lo crea una persona y lo aprovecha todo el equipo. [Más información.](https://www.notion.com/help/custom-agent)

¿Cuál es la diferencia entre los agentes personalizados y el agente de Notion?

Los [agentes personalizados](https://www.notion.com/help/custom-agent)
 son ayudantes de IA para todo el equipo que funcionan automáticamente siguiendo una frecuencia o un disparador. El [agente de Notion](https://www.notion.com/help/personal-agent)
 es un asistente personal de IA que actúa cuando tú lo pides. Todos los usuarios de Notion tienen acceso al agente de Notion. Los clientes de los planes Business y Enterprise pueden usar agentes personalizados, y su uso se factura según el sistema de créditos de Notion.

¿Quién puede crear agentes personalizados?

Cualquier persona con un plan Business o Enterprise, incluidos los periodos de prueba de Business, tiene la función de crear agentes personalizados de forma predeterminada. Los administradores de Business y Enterprise pueden limitar quién puede crearlos desde el panel de administración.

¿Qué herramientas e integraciones son compatibles con los agentes personalizados?

**Slack:** lee y publica mensajes en canales públicos. Activa agentes con reacciones de emoji y menciones. Próximamente estarán disponibles los canales privados.

**Mail**: lee, organiza y redacta correos de forma automática. Los agentes pueden aplicar etiquetas, sincronizar correos con bases de datos de Notion y activarse con disparadores como la llegada de nuevos mensajes de remitentes concretos. [Más información.](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/guides/manage-your-inbox-and-calendar-with-custom-agents)

**Calendar**: consulta tu agenda, encuentra huecos para reuniones y crea o actualiza eventos. Los agentes pueden prepararte para las reuniones, coordinar la disponibilidad entre participantes y activarse cuando se crea, modifica o cancela un evento. [Más información.](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/guides/manage-your-inbox-and-calendar-with-custom-agents)

**Notion MCP**: conéctate a apps externas mediante el protocolo de contexto de modelo. Utiliza integraciones de socios ya configuradas, como Linear, Figma, HubSpot, Ramp, Wiz, Stripe, GitHub, Intercom, Amplitude, Attio y Sentry. También puedes conectarte a cualquier servidor MCP personalizado (incluidas herramientas internas) mediante la conexión MCP personalizada. [Más información.](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/guides/connect-custom-agents-to-mcp-integrations)

¿Qué pueden controlar los administradores con los agentes personalizados?

Los administradores de equipos con planes Business y Enterprise tienen visibilidad y control sobre cómo se utilizan los agentes personalizados en su espacio de trabajo. Pueden decidir quién puede crearlos, a qué tiene acceso cada agente y deshabilitarlos en cualquier momento. Cada ejecución queda registrada, de modo que los cambios son visibles y se pueden deshacer.

**Gestiona quién puede crear agentes.** Configura los permisos de creación en Configuración → IA de Notion.

**Deshabilita los agentes en cualquier momento.** Detén todas las ejecuciones, ediciones y chats de cualquier agente.

**Consulta todos los agentes del espacio de trabajo y sus accesos.** Revisa cada agente, a qué puede acceder y quién lo ha creado.

**Supervisa el uso de créditos de Notion.** Controla el consumo en tiempo real, identifica qué agentes utilizan más créditos y recibe avisos al llegar al 80 % y al 100 %.

¿Están seguros mis datos con los agentes personalizados?

Sí. Los agentes respetan tus permisos, cada ejecución queda registrada y todos los cambios se pueden deshacer. Notion no usa tu contenido para entrenar sus modelos de IA. Además, en los planes Enterprise no se conservan los datos.

¿Cuánto cuestan los agentes personalizados?

A partir del 4 de mayo de 2026, los agentes personalizados funcionarán con créditos de Notion, disponibles como complemento de los planes Business y Enterprise. Cuanto más trabajo hagan por ti, más créditos consumirán.

Los créditos mensuales de Notion cuestan 10 USD por cada 1000 créditos. Puedes comprar la cantidad que necesites, desde unos cientos hasta varios miles. Se comparten en todo el espacio de trabajo y se reinician cada mes.

Si tienes un equipo de cuenta, podrá ayudarte a elegir la cantidad de créditos más adecuada para un mayor volumen de uso, con opciones flexibles como créditos anuales o bajo demanda.

¿Cómo funcionan los créditos de Notion?

Los créditos de Notion se utilizan para ejecutar agentes personalizados y están disponibles como complemento en los planes Business y Enterprise. La cantidad de créditos que consume un agente personalizado depende de la tarea: las más sencillas requieren menos, mientras que los flujos de trabajo más complejos y con varios pasos consumen más. [Más información.](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/custom-agent-pricing)

Los créditos mensuales de Notion se usan en todo el espacio de trabajo y se reinician cada mes. Los créditos no utilizados no se acumulan para el mes siguiente. Puedes consultar opciones adicionales de créditos con el equipo de Ventas.

El resto de las funciones con IA (el agente de Notion, el Anotador con IA y la Búsqueda Enterprise) están incluidas en los planes Business y Enterprise sin coste adicional.

Modo Investigación: la búsqueda que trabaja por ti
--------------------------------------------------

Crea informes detallados en cuestión de minutos que puedes guardar y compartir, cuyos datos extrae de todas tus fuentes y de la web.

![Resultados de investigación](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F4EGD4mbwhwiuZE3Tr4FDLs%2F6f78054470df24727c0664a44af04054%2Fresearch-hero.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Te ahorra días de tiempo

Analiza tus espacios de trabajo, apps e incluso la web en minutos.

### Piensa a fondo

Mira cómo la IA de Notion descompone cada pregunta en un proceso de investigación paso a paso.

### Escribe informes listos para compartir

Obtén informes pulidos y completos que puedes guardar y compartir al instante sin trabajo adicional.

Nunca empieces un documento desde cero
--------------------------------------

Crea actualizaciones de proyectos a partir de fuentes dispersas
---------------------------------------------------------------

Crea resúmenes semanales de progreso y bloqueos, incluyendo información de últimos tickets de Jira, PRs de GitHub y conversaciones del equipo en Slack o Microsoft Teams.

![Indicación de investigación (compacta)](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2FItLiQf9EE33q7AMNFJJxF%2Fc3d0006d9696bc984cc2dd54b6a2b22e%2Fresearch-prompt.png&w=3840&q=75)

Informes sobre tus clientes en cuestión de minutos
--------------------------------------------------

Acelera el desarrollo de producto con un feedback más rápido. El Modo Investigación analiza llamadas de investigación, tickets de Zendesk (próximamente) y detecta comentarios relevantes en toda la web.

![Investigación en curso (compacta)](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F255Ia0chnCH3Rqa7pXIqvC%2F33c0ad10c5ba536e51bbdef8041f3f79%2Fresearch-researching.png&w=3840&q=75)

Empieza cada reunión con ventaja
--------------------------------

¿Tienes una llamada con un cliente? El Modo Investigación reúne información competitiva a partir de documentos internos, la web y Salesforce (próximamente) para que siempre vayas dos pasos por delante.

![Resultados de la investigación (compacto)](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F1rXSZGqjWffhXsr9wsPIOw%2F3b678ba38b01b517eaea1c91c376c34c%2Fresearch-results.png&w=3840&q=75)

Busca y analiza a tu manera
---------------------------

### Elige tus modelos de IA

Empieza a chatear con tus modelos de IA preferidos directamente desde tu espacio de trabajo. Sin coste adicional y sin que tus datos se utilicen para entrenarlos.

![Selecciona el modelo que prefieras](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F4lWamvavoqCkOLeJHyapvV%2F616d808b20690b428e4c1e33e1ebc7a5%2Fmodel-picker.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Busca en tus PDF

La IA de Notion busca en los PDF que se han subido al espacio de trabajo y a Google Drive, SharePoint y OneDrive.

![Búsqueda en la app del móvil](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F6yX6yWkwC5mn50VygkNhUM%2Fcd8795f85582904e8dd2e8b03159fb0d%2Fimage.png&w=3840&q=75)

Busca de forma segura
---------------------

[Más información sobre seguridad y privacidad](https://www.notion.com/help/enterprise-search-security-and-privacy-practices)

![Ilustración: Trusted 2](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F3tR3vMeWqqg0CopRiaAOdy%2Fc633f156505729d0c2756bbea8f4830c%2FMetaphoric-Spots_AccessControls_blue_2.png&w=1920&q=75)

### Respeta la configuración de permisos

La IA de Notion muestra solo la información a la que tú, como usuario, tienes permiso de acceso, incluyendo todas tus apps conectadas.

### Tus datos no se usan para entrenar a la IA

Tenemos acuerdos contractuales con nuestros subprocesadores de IA que prohíben el uso de los datos de los clientes para entrenar sus modelos.

### Controla dónde buscas

Tú eliges las apps, fuentes (como la web) y modelos de IA que quieres usar para hacer la búsqueda, por lo que tienes el control total.

### Cifrado seguro

Cuando utilizas la IA de Notion, tus datos se cifran en tránsito utilizando TLS 1.2 o superior.

### Cumple con las normas de seguridad y cumplimiento

SOC 2 (Tipo 2), ISO 27001, RGPD, CCPA y sin conservación de datos (solo plan Enterprise).

![Insignias de seguridad ](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2FE5mmSJW2NMzreRHu59eQ9%2F4c1a473f6a7a851f0ac8490624a4c260%2FEnterprise_Search_-_security_badges_3.png&w=1920&q=75)

Preguntas y respuestas
----------------------

¿Cómo busca la IA de Notion en múltiples apps?

Mediante las conexiones de IA, la IA de Notion ejecuta búsquedas de conocimiento interno indexando el contenido de tus herramientas de trabajo según tus permisos. Cuando haces una pregunta, busca mensajes en Slack; archivos y PDF en Google Drive; tickets de Jira; incidencias y solicitudes de extracción en GitHub; y otras apps conectadas, para ofrecerte la información más relevante con rapidez.

¿Qué herramientas puedo conectar a la IA de Notion?

Ahora puedes integrar apps como Slack, Google Drive, GitHub, Jira, MSFT Teams, SharePoint, OneDrive. Pronto se sumarán otras como Linear, Gmail, Salesforce, Zendesk, Box y más. Estas integraciones permiten una verdadera experiencia de búsqueda unificada en todas tus fuentes de conocimiento internas y externas.

¿Es seguro usar la IA de Notion?

Sí. La IA de Notion solo muestra la información a la que tienes permiso de acceso. Además, cumple con estrictos estándares de seguridad como SOC 2 Tipo 2, ISO 27001, RGPD y cumplimiento de CCPA, sin conservación de datos para usuarios del plan Enterprise. Descubre [cómo protegemos la seguridad y la privacidad en la Búsqueda Enterprise](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/enterprise-search-security-and-privacy-practices.)

¿Puede la IA de Notion crear informes a partir de múltiples fuentes?

Sí. Con el Modo Investigación, la IA de Notion analiza datos de tus apps conectadas y la web para generar informes detallados que pueden compartirse al instante. Esto les ahorra a los equipos días y días de búsqueda manual.

¿Puedo elegir en qué fuentes busca la IA de Notion?

Sí. Tú decides dónde quieres que busque la IA de Notion al seleccionar qué apps, documentos y fuentes web incluir, además de la forma en la que lo hace, por lo que tienes el control total.

¿En qué se diferencia la IA de Notion de las herramientas de búsqueda corporativas tradicionales?

A diferencia de la búsqueda tradicional, la IA de Notion no solo encuentra archivos, sino que entiende preguntas, recupera respuestas actualizadas con citas e incluso utiliza el pensamiento crítico para analizar preguntas complejas y generar informes de investigación detallados en minutos.

FAQs
----

![](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=%2Ffront-static%2Fpages%2Ftemplates%2Fcategory-FAQ.png&w=256&q=75)

Does Notion support project templates for different industries?

Yes, Notion offers project templates for various industries, from software and marketing to construction and education. Each template can be customized to fit industry-specific workflows while maintaining core project management principles.

Do Notion project management tools allow custom workflow creation?

Yes. Notion's composable approach lets you create custom workflows tailored to your team's needs, combining different views and properties that can evolve as your projects change.

What does "composable project management" mean?

It's the idea of building your system from modular parts that can be reconfigured as needs change. Your project management tool, built by you, for you.

Is Notion good for project management?

Yes. Teams use Notion to manage plans, tasks, timelines, docs, and status updates in one place. Because templates are composable, you can tailor workflows (Agile, Waterfall, hybrid) without duct‑taping multiple tools together. Competitors offer templates too, but Notion's linked databases keep everything connected.

What project management templates should I start with?

Start with a project plan, timeline (Gantt), WBS, RACI, and a weekly status report. These together cover the four fundamentals of any project: scope, schedule, ownership, and communication.

Can I manage Agile projects in Notion?

Yes. Use a backlog and sprint board (Kanban), plus a timeline for capacity planning. Add retrospectives and a change log to complete the loop.

How do Notion templates compare to spreadsheets or docs?

Templates in spreadsheets are quick, but they're usually static. Notion templates create databases you can relate, filter, and visualize (board, timeline, calendar), with the flexibility to adapt as projects grow. Notion lets you bring docs, tasks, and wiki together in one space. No more SaaS sprawl!

New tools, new ways to work
---------------------------

### We also built in some advanced features for you.

Sign up

![An animation of a Notion workspace’s sidebar with multiple levels of nested entries](https://www.notion.com/front-static/pages/evernote/features/infinite-hierarchy-v2.gif)

### Infinite hierarchy

No limits on nesting pages inside pages for better organization.

![A screenshot of a Notion table database filled with multiple rows and columns of content](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=%2Ffront-static%2Fpages%2Fevernote%2Ffeatures%2Ftables-v2.png&w=1920&q=75)

### Tables & databases

Keep simple or sophisticated records with views, filters, tags, and more.

![A screenshot of a popup menu appearing after a slash containining blocks text can be transformed in to](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=%2Ffront-static%2Fshared%2Ffeatures%2Fmarkdown%2Fen-US.png&w=1920&q=75)

### #Markdown & /slash commands

Access all of Notion’s tools without touching your mouse to stay in flow.

![An animation showing how easy it is to drag and drop content](https://www.notion.com/front-static/shared/features/drag-and-drop-v2/en-US.gif)

### Drag & drop

Get your ideas on the page, then rearrange. Our editor helps you structure your thoughts and plans.

# Notion Demo Hub

Featured use cases
------------------

Here are some of our most popular features and use cases to get you started.

### Build a project reporting Custom Agent

Let a Notion Custom Agent automatically summarize project updates and share them to Slack.

[Start tour→](https://demo.hellonotion.com/psl/custom-agent-weekly-update)

![Notion's Agent automatically shares project updates](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F2x2z1UIXMVOJgaQ9uOgxkA%2Fea614dcba1d02c4467fadec5b75049d5%2FScreenshot_2026-03-16_at_2.15.46%C3%A2__PM.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Build a bug triaging Custom Agent

Questions & Answers
-------------------

How do I start using AI Meeting Notes in Notion?

To start, type `/meet` on any Notion page, join a meeting from your Notion Calendar, or Notion will send a gentle reminder when it automatically detects meetings. AI Meeting Notes will begin capturing your meeting and generate an organized summary as soon as the meeting’s over.

Does AI Meeting Notes work with Zoom, Google Meet, and Microsoft Teams?

Yes! AI Meeting Notes in Notion records system audio, so you can capture Zoom meetings, Google Meet calls, and Teams meeting—no bots or extra software required.

Can AI Meeting Notes create action items automatically?

Absolutely. Notion's AI analyzes your meeting transcript to generate summaries and action items, saving your team hours of manual work.

How fast are the summaries available after a meeting?

AI Meeting Notes generates summaries instantly after the meeting ends—no waiting. Your team can put action items to work right away.

Can I search across past meeting notes?

Yes! Every transcript, summary, decision, and action item is saved in Notion and fully searchable across your workspace using Notion AI.

Is my meeting data secure?

Yes. You control exactly who can see your meeting notes and transcripts. Plus, Notion provides built-in privacy settings and one-click consent collection before meetings start.

Why use Notion’s AI Meeting Notes instead of other meeting note apps?

Unlike standalone apps, AI Meeting Notes lives directly in your Notion workspace—meaning your notes, tasks, and projects stay seamlessly connected. No switching tools, no lost context.

What languages does AI Meeting Notes support?

AI Meeting Notes supports 19 languages including English, French, Japanese and more, with three additional languages in Beta.

Can I use AI Meeting Notes for any type of meeting?

Yes, you can use AI Meeting Notes for any meeting! Whether it's a 1:1s, team sync, sales calls, AI will create a helpful summary based on the context to fit your needs.

What should I look out for when buying meeting notes products?

It’s a complicated market–check out our handy [buyer’s guide](https://www.notion.com/product/ai-meeting-notes/ai-meeting-software-buyers-guide)
 for a breakdown on what to look out for.

Featured Story

Clay’s New Default: Workflows That Happen in the Background

An editor designed for focus.
-----------------------------

Just start typing. Everything else fades away so you can concentrate on the task at hand-no distractions.

![Pen illustration](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F7nhSBMG8f49XYhOPWOi0V9%2F6d7247bf5ac4e14a1bd764053af74b46%2Fpen.webp&w=1080&q=75)

### Markdown-friendly & keyboard-first

Type "/" for a list or "#" for a heading—stay in flow without touching your mouse.

![Page editor](https://images.ctfassets.net/spoqsaf9291f/UwaLFFB1lBH9mXZGlJwtO/4e02639894f698815ab953c687b86ce5/notes-editor-en-us.gif)

Re-order blocks, embed Looms, or drop spreadsheets right next to your notes with a simple drag.

![Drag and Drop UI](https://images.ctfassets.net/spoqsaf9291f/ncH6Mw9fvgNjUwbuUelaR/d4ea8f6950a96e830e9f64c329f51c04/darg-and-drop.gif)

### Many types of content

Add images, bookmarks, videos, code, and more without touching your mouse. Stay in the flow.

![Block Types Animation](https://images.ctfassets.net/spoqsaf9291f/6xQNq60dNQiJkivkigkSlW/fa5b4452883b71bb68e9b3705594b15c/slash-commands.gif)

Organize your notes your way.
-----------------------------

Notion is more than a text editor. Use powerful databases to categorize meeting notes, tag teammates, set due dates, and connect them to projects.

![Pen illustration](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2FaFzOEOD3xueO4CMbYNJVW%2F73e45a9211eed5391023caa61cc7b72f%2Fpost-its.png&w=1080&q=75)

### Turn notes into tasks

Convert any bullet into an actionable task and track it in Kanban board, a calendar, or a timeline view.

![Connected apps](https://images.ctfassets.net/spoqsaf9291f/5bXxrcTu7UdV1Xol6fao7y/732df778f6116102e0d24cdfa56098d9/meeting-notes-views.gif)

Never lose track of a note again. Everything lives in the sidebar for immediate access.

![Connected apps](https://images.ctfassets.net/spoqsaf9291f/5WyF5X3vJ6fILIorBJLIP8/87fa199e9ca079842d178806ad02c930/sidebar-nesting.gif)

Define and add your own tags. Organize your information the way you want to work.

--------------------------------

Multiple teammates typing in the same note? No problem. Cursor presence shows who’s editing.

Questions & answers
-------------------

How do I take meeting notes quickly?

Type `/meet` during your call or open the Meeting Notes template from the sidebar. Notion AI starts capturing instantly. [Learn more about AI Meeting Notes here.](https://www.notion.com/product/ai-meeting-notes)

Can I import notes from Evernote or Google Docs?

Yes, our importers allow you to bring existing content into Notion in one click.

Are my notes secure?

All data is encrypted in transit (TLS 1.2+) and at rest (AES-256). You control sharing permissions at the page or workspace level.

What makes Notion different from other note-taking apps?

Notion combines notes, docs, databases, and AI in one flexible workspace. Unlike traditional note apps, you can turn any note into a task, connect it to projects, and collaborate in real-time—all without switching tools..

What should be included in meeting notes?

Stick to the must-haves: agenda topic → key points → decisions → action items with owners and due dates. Anything else can live in sub-pages or comments.

# Notion Security & Compliance | SOC 2 Certified, trusted by Enterprises

Security
--------

Notion takes a security-by-design approach to protecting your data. Our team continues to make investments so you can use Notion with confidence.

[Our security practices →](https://www.notion.com/help/security-and-privacy)

![Spot Illustration: Lock key holes - Blue](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F7dU3O8gnlsIkhli1vq4p7D%2Fd4b38bed30a4992f9e6139c7d394eb8c%2FLock_key_holes.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Security infrastructure

Notion’s infrastructure is designed with layers of protection to help ensure your data is secure while transmitted, stored, or processed. Protections include but are not limited to encryption, least privilege access, secure software development, and a public bug bounty program.

[Submit Vulnerability Report→](https://hackerone.com/b21888db-e0d1-48cd-b61b-55aaa96600d4/embedded_submissions/new)

### Operational security

Our information security team continuously implements new security controls and monitors Notion for malicious activity across our infrastructure, networks, and assets.

### Product security

Notion provides a robust set of in product data protection and admin controls for greater visibility and control over our data. Enterprise admins can deploy Notion to their organizations with SSO via SAML 2.0, provision users through SCIM, and track activity with the audit log features. Enterprise admins can also fine tune permission controls and guests, and manage team organizations.

Privacy
-------

Notion maintains a comprehensive privacy compliance program and is committed to partnering with its customers and vendors on privacy compliance efforts.

![Spot Illustration: Dog at fence - blue](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F2YwomD27oPDl5M4Xkve6CD%2F7b356526cbd9e8cb2e0b16a3533bb071%2FDog_at_fence.png&w=1920&q=75)

### How we handle your data

At Notion our team is dedicated to developing and implementing data privacy processes and safeguards that meet industry standards and best practices. We conduct ongoing training for our teams to ensure that they are up to speed with developments in legislation and essential privacy and security practices. Every Notion employee and contractor signs up to non-disclosure terms to maintain the confidentiality and security of your data. Notion also holds any vendors that handle personal data to the same data management, security, and privacy practices and standards to which we hold ourselves.

### Agreements

At Notion we strive to keep all of our agreements up to date with the latest regulations and industry standards. Our Master Subscription Agreement and Data Processing Addendum describe in detail Notion’s data privacy processes, standards, safeguards and our compliance with data protection legislation. To ensure that our terms track with the GDPR, CCPA and other global privacy standards we continually have our terms assessed by leading privacy experts in multiple jurisdictions.

### Data governance

Data governance relates to the policies and procedures that dictate how data is procured and used throughout its life cycle. From creation and collection to processing, distribution, storage and deletion. Notion’s commitment to data governance is key to keeping our users data secure, private, accurate, and accessible.

### GDPR

The General Data Protection Regulation (GDPR) is a comprehensive data protection law that governs the collection of and use of personal data of EU residents, and that allows data subjects to exercise control over their data. As the GDPR is widely considered to be the most stringent global privacy standard, we have mapped our privacy program to the GDPR and other global privacy regulations.

### Policies

At Notion we want to be as transparent as possible with our customers about how we collect, process, store, and use their personal data. In order to achieve this Notion maintains comprehensive and detailed policies regarding how we handle your personal information. These policies describe in detail how our users can exercise their rights with regard to their data.

[Our terms & privacy policy→](https://notion.notion.site/Terms-and-Privacy-28ffdd083dc3473e9c2da6ec011b58ac)

Compliance
----------

Notion maintains a comprehensive security and privacy program to provide advanced security features in our Enterprise plan that are designed to protect your data in accordance with various regulatory and industry standards. Notion has been attested by independent third-party auditors. If you’d like a copy of the compliance reports, please visit our Trust Center.

[Our Trust Center →](https://trust.notion.com/)

![Spot illustration: blueprints - blue ](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F6IOcGytvQ506uybKVbMxfH%2F350f6b83d12fb002a620db7d5fc66583%2Fpaper.png&w=3840&q=75)

### SOC 2 Type 2

The SOC 2 Type 2 is an audit report performed by an independent third-party certified by the American Institute of Certified Public Accountants (AICPA) to evaluate a service organization's controls related to the Trust Services Criteria (TSC). The SOC 2 Type 2 report assesses the effectiveness of these controls over a period of time and is intended to provide assurance to customers and stakeholders that the organization has implemented adequate controls to protect their data.

![Acme Inc company wiki](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F1FWv4AhXkSZRRKhXqrGE9a%2Fccda9dfe1fbb3acdbd3ac7b526fa8901%2Fsecurity-compliance-soc-2-type-2.png&w=1920&q=75)

### ISO 27001, ISO 27701, ISO 27017, ISO 27018

ISO is an international standard development organization, and Notion has achieved certifications for four ISO standards: ISO 27001, ISO 27701, ISO 27017, and ISO 27018. The standards outline requirements for establishing, implementing, and continuously improving Notion’s Information Security Management System (ISMS) and Privacy Information Management System (PIMS).

![Acme Inc company wiki](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F1PtvQNjLzIHOV1BdEsZwiJ%2F82e5046b08dbcf1610d4786d2d3ac2da%2Fsecurity-compliance-iso-v2.png&w=1920&q=75)

### HIPAA

The Health Insurance Portability and Accountability Act (HIPAA) is a US federal law that was enacted in 1996 that requires the protection and confidential handling of protected health information (PHI) by covered entities such as healthcare providers, health plans, and healthcare clearinghouses, as well as their business associates. Provided businesses subject to HIPAA leverage the Notion Enterprise-grade security features described in our Help Center article here and sign Notion’s Business Associate Agreement they may process PHI within their Notion workspace.

![Acme Inc company wiki](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F2quoFJCv2s9b91owAwVLDJ%2Fb0ff0f0f09b1ae6806338b19cadb15cc%2Fsecurity-compliance-hipaa.png&w=1920&q=75)

### BSI C5 (Cloud Computing Compliance Controls Catalogue)

BSI C5 is a security standard developed by the German Federal Office for Information Security. It outlines baseline security controls for cloud service providers. C5 includes additional control requirements relating to data location, service provisioning, place of jurisdiction, existing certifications, information disclosure obligations, and a full-service description.

![Acme Inc company wiki](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F3naUmSpP61tu3yD4IBUQAI%2F23f28dbd3ad3d56b244f06bd8ab8c5a9%2Fsecurity-compliance-bsi-c5.png&w=1920&q=75)

Artificial intelligence (AI) governance
---------------------------------------

Notion leverages AI to improve the core product experience and provide real value to our users in their day-to-day work. We strive to do this in a way that’s trustworthy, reliable, and user-centric.

![Spot Illustration: Rubik's cube - blue](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F658mqE8zbJjnsY8JSn5tLo%2F50f71d586babc9e69a12a27ad718b127%2FRubik-s_cube.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Safe & secure

Notion takes a safety-first approach to artificial intelligence. Our AI features and partners undergo security and legal reviews prior to Notion utilizing their services. These security practices apply to our AI features and AI development process.

[Our security practices→](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-ai-security-practices)

### Transparency

At Notion, we want to be transparent with our customers about our AI products. In order to achieve this Notion maintains a Help Center and Terms and Privacy page to outline how our AI products’ functionality and privacy practices.

[Our terms & privacy policy→](https://app.notion.com/p/notion/Terms-and-Privacy-28ffdd083dc3473e9c2da6ec011b58ac)

### Empowering

We aim to create AI-enhanced experiences that aren’t just interesting — but rather, genuinely useful in your day-to-day work. To achieve this, the development of our AI-powered features is grounded in extensive research to understand the needs of our users.

### Data governance

Your data is yours. Our AI Subprocessors are prohibited from using Customer Data to train models. The controls and permissions with respect to access and use of customer data will be respected.

Reliability
-----------

Notion is relied on from creatives to cooperations - as such, everyone deserves a platform they can count on. With robust uptime guarantees and multi-level redundancy, you can trust Notion will be there when you need it.

![Spot Illustration: Flexible tools pocket knife - Blue](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2FZmLtxhnUafKBGJyXJeK6Q%2F793cfb07fd456f1b293ac25e6e45c5d0%2Fflexible-tool.png&w=3840&q=75)

### High availability & Failover

Notion keeps your data safe by having multiple zones for redundancy, have a comprehensive backup program, and regularly testing our disaster recovery and business continuity program. Notion offers a guaranteed uptime of 99.9%, so users can trust that we’ll be there when you need us.

[Service level terms→](https://notion.notion.site/Service-Level-Terms-6f805fa1d4ca4463b805e2832ae8ff0d)

### Enterprise-grade Infrastructure

We partner with AWS and Cloudflare to build a world-class architecture and to ensure users that Notion is built for maximum business resilience.

### Service Status

Notion makes it transparent and easy with a real-time view of Notion’s availability through the status page.

[Status page→](https://www.notion-status.com/)

Learn about our enterprise plan
-------------------------------

Interested in advanced security and control? Let us know your needs and we can help!

[Get Notion free](https://www.notion.com/signup)
[Request a demo](https://www.notion.com/contact-sales)

# Join Notion Solutions Partner Program | Notion

One program. Two tracks.
------------------------

![Scaffolding illustration](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F1RotvrvgavvdtZS1kWsAjh%2Fd0477d17a67874c980cc7ffde20db380%2FScaffolding.png&w=1920&q=75)

### Consulting Partner

Refer clients to Notion. Lead the implementation. Deliver ongoing services.

*   What you do:
*   Source and qualify opportunities with clients who can benefit from Notion
    
*   Co-sell alongside Notion to design and scope the right solution
    
*   Deliver and manage implementations that drive adoption and measurable outcomes
    
*   Support customer growth through ongoing optimization and change management
    
*   Ideal for systems integrators, agencies, and consultants focused on delivery, outcomes, and expansion
    

[Become a Consulting Partner→](https://www.notion.so/profile/services)

### Channel Partner

Resell Notion. Implement with confidence. Drive renewal and expansion.

*   What you do:
*   Resell Notion
    
*   Handle procurement/fulfillment
    
*   Implement, train, and drive expansion/renewal
    
*   Ideal for resellers, VARs, MSPs, and sales-led consultancies with a services bench focused on new lands and expansion
    

[Become a Channel Partner→](https://www.notion.so/profile/services)

![Notion logo](https://images.ctfassets.net/spoqsaf9291f/1XDrBlBhttaDBW7OsSIHVJ/0a86cf7c5a22e558fa724f691dfa6c02/affirm-logo-color.svg)

**Nora Grasham**Senior Director, IT Engineering

Leading companies get faster business results with an expert partner.
---------------------------------------------------------------------

From startups to enterprises, companies all around the world have turned Notion into working systems that scale with certified experts guiding the way.

[See how](https://www.notion.com/customers/solutions-partners)

![Collaboration illustration](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F5SqcMNkFc0BZI2gs0ozAFi%2F981b2e82ba2c1cd8a18aca84a792f1ec%2FMetaphoric-Spots_collaboration2_blue_2.png&w=1920&q=75)

Questions & answers
-------------------

What’s the process to become a Solutions Partner?

The first step is to create your partner profile, accept the Solutions Partner Agreement, and submit your application. Our team will review it, and once approved, you’ll be eligible to complete the required certifications to become a Solutions Partner. [Get started here.](https://www.notion.so/profile/services)

My application was approved, what should I do next?

Once you’re approved, your next step is to complete the required certifications for your track. Passing these will unlock your badges and credentials and officially confirm your status as a Solutions Partner. After that, you’ll just need to finalize your profile so you can be listed in the directory.

What does it take to become a successful partner?

Successful partners build a focused Notion practice around their strengths. They invest in certifications, package repeatable offerings, deliver measurable outcomes, and execute consistently. Explore partner stories [here](https://www.notion.com/customers/solutions-partners)
 to get inspired.

I am a company looking to hire a Solutions Partner, how do I get started?

Start by browsing the [partner directory](https://www.notion.com/solutions-partners)
. Look for partners who serve your region and language and provide the type of work you need. Once you’ve found a good match, reach out to schedule a discovery call to explore fit.

What is the difference between a Sales Partner and a Consulting Partner?

We have two partner types in the Solutions Partner Program: Sales Partners and Consulting Partners.

*   Sales Partners focus on driving revenue through activities like sourcing new customers, facilitating expansions, managing renewals, and providing account oversight.
    
*   Consulting Partners help customers adopt and scale with Notion by delivering services such as consulting, implementation, integrations, training, or ongoing managed support.
    

A partner can take on one or both roles. Each type also has its own tiers, with distinct benefits and requirements.

# Notion Web Clipper for Chrome, Safari, Firefox, and mobile

Notion Web Clipper
==================

Save any page on the web to Notion. We’ll help you turn them into action.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
