Notion Creator & Consultant

What is Marketplace?

Marketplace is a place for Notion users to discover templates and get inspired by what’s possible in Notion. Templates in Marketplace are made by Notion’s community of experts, designers, and people just like you.

What is a template?

A template is a pre-designed page (or set of pages) that Notion users can duplicate and customize for their own workflows and needs.

Who can list and sell templates on Marketplace?

Anyone can create a template and list it on Marketplace! All templates are reviewed by the Notion team before they are officially listed in Marketplace.

La IA que funciona donde trabaja tu equipo. Pruébala gratis.
------------------------------------------------------------

### Gratuito

Para que todo el mundo organice su día a día y sus proyectos personales.

[Registrarse](https://www.notion.com/signup)

**Incluye:**

*   Prueba las funciones de IA como la generación de documentos o el autocompletado en las bases de datos
    
    Periodo de prueba de la IA de Notion
    
*   Captura, organiza y actúa en función de las respuestas directamente desde Notion.
    
    Formularios básicos
    
*   Publica una página de Notion en la web
    
    Sitios básicos
    
*   Conecta múltiples calendarios para gestionar tu tiempo y tu trabajo en un mismo lugar.
    
    Notion Calendar
    
*   Conecta tu cuenta de Gmail para obtener una bandeja de entrada personalizada con IA.
    
    Notion Mail (se sincroniza con Gmail)
    
*   Organiza cientos o miles de elementos en un solo lugar, como los proyectos o las tareas
    
    Bases de datos que incluyen subtareas, dependencias, propiedades personalizadas y mucho más
    

### BusinessRecomendación

Para que las empresas en crecimiento agilicen el trabajo en equipo.

[Empezar](https://www.notion.com/signup?target=plans)

**Todo lo que incluye el plan Plus, más:**

*   Trabaja para ti. Realiza tareas complejas de varios pasos utilizando el contexto de Notion, tus aplicaciones conectadas y la web.
    
    Agente de Notion
    
*   Los agentes de IA gestionan tareas repetitivas de forma autónoma para que tu equipo no tenga que hacerlo. Pruébalos gratis. Luego te costarán 10 $ por cada 1000 créditos.
    
    Agentes personalizados
    
*   Automatiza las notas y los seguimientos de tus reuniones sin necesidad de bots
    
    Anotador con IA
    
*   Busca en aplicaciones conectadas como Slack y GitHub, entre otras
    
    Búsqueda EnterpriseBeta
    
*   Gestiona el acceso de los empleados a gran escala con el inicio de sesión único (SSO) seguro.
    
    Inicio de sesión único de SAML
    
*   Trabaja en equipo en una base de datos de Notion sin dar acceso a toda ella. En su lugar, limítalo a las filas en las que se asigna al colaborador.
    
    Permisos de base de datos específicos
    
*   Añade una insignia de verificación a las páginas que estén actualizadas. La insignia aparecerá en los resultados de búsqueda y en las citas de IA.
    
    Verifica páginas
    
*   Crea espacios de equipo que nadie pueda ver ni encontrar a excepción de quienes tú añadas. Ideal para tratar información confidencial, como la planificación empresarial o las evaluaciones de rendimiento.
    
    Espacios de equipo privados
    
*   Verifica la titularidad de un dominio de correo electrónico para acceder a funciones de seguridad avanzada, como el inicio de sesión único.
    
    Verificación de dominios
    
*   Conéctate a GitHub, Asana y mucho más
    
    Conexiones prémium

### Personaliza permisos

Tú controlas lo que la IA de Notion puede ver y hacer.

[Más información sobre prácticas de seguridad →](https://www.notion.so/help/notion-ai-security-practices?_gl=1*p1njrn*_gcl_au*MTcxMjUyNjE2LjE3NDQ4MTY4MzM.*_ga*MTgyNjkyNzg0MS4xNzI5MTA5MzMx*_ga_9ZJ8CB186L*MTc0NjA0NDM5Mi4yMzcuMS4xNzQ2MDQ1Njk5LjUwLjAuMA..)

### Tus datos no se usan para entrenar a la IA

Tenemos acuerdos contractuales con subprocesadores de IA que prohíben el uso de datos de clientes para entrenar sus modelos.

### SOC 2 (Tipo 2) e ISO 27001

Notion se compromete a cumplir con los estándares más altos de seguridad de la información.

### RGPD y CCPA

Hemos alineado nuestro programa de privacidad con el RGPD y otras normativas globales de protección de datos.

### Cifrado seguro

Cuando utilizas la IA de Notion, tus datos se cifran en tránsito utilizando TLS 1.2 o superior.

### Cero conservación de datos en el plan Enterprise

No se almacena ningún dato con los proveedores de modelos de lenguaje. Conservación de 30 días para planes que no son Enterprise.

[Contacta con Ventas ->→](https://www.notion.com/es-es/contact-sales)

### Cumplimiento con la ley HIPAA en el plan Enterprise

La IA de Notion permite cumplir la HIPAA utilizando las API de retención cero de los proveedores de LLM y permite procesar información de salud protegida (PHI).

[Contacta con Ventas ->→](https://www.notion.com/es-es/contact-sales)

Preguntas y respuestas
----------------------

¿Qué puede ayudarme a hacer la IA de Notion?

La IA de Notion es tu compañero de equipo integrado en Notion y trabaja directamente en tus páginas, documentos, tareas y bases de datos para que puedas moverte más rápido sin cambiar de herramienta. Usando el contexto de tu espacio de trabajo y de las apps conectadas (cuando están habilitadas), te ayuda a sacar trabajo adelante a partir de tus ideas, todo en un solo lugar.

**Esto es lo que puedes hacer con la IA de Notion:**

*   Chatea con el [**agente de Notion**](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/notion-ai-faqs#personal-agent)
     para que se encargue de tareas de principio a fin, utilizando el contexto de tu espacio de trabajo y de las apps conectadas para crear y editar páginas y bases de datos.
    
*   Utiliza los [**agentes personalizados**](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/custom-agent)
     para automatizar el trabajo recurrente de tu equipo, por ejemplo, para responder a preguntas en Slack, asignar tareas y compartir actualizaciones de los proyectos.
    
*   Busca en tu espacio de trabajo y en las apps conectadas, como Slack y Google Drive, con la [**Búsqueda Enterprise**](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/notion-ai-faqs#enterprise-search)
     y las [**conexiones de la IA de Notion**](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/notion-ai-connectors)
     para encontrar respuestas sin tener que cambiar de herramienta.
    
*   Registra las reuniones con el [**Anotador con IA**](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/notion-ai-faqs#ai-meeting-notes-(beta))
    , que transcribe las conversaciones, resume los puntos clave y extrae información automáticamente.
    
*   Profundiza en un tema con el [**Modo Investigación**](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/notion-ai-faqs#research-mode)
     para generar informes y resúmenes detallados.
    
*   Mejora la redacción o genera borradores con [**bloques de IA**](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/notion-ai-faqs#notion-ai-inline)
     directamente en tus páginas.
    
*   Crea [**bases de datos**](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/notion-ai-faqs#notion-ai-for-databases)
    , rellena propiedades con[**Autocompletado**](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/autofill#autofill)
    , y usa fórmulas para crear flujos de trabajo y automatizaciones más inteligentes.
    

Para asegurar un rendimiento óptimo y un uso justo para todos, el acceso a las funciones de la IA de Notion puede reducirse temporalmente según el uso individual.

¿Qué son los agentes personalizados?

Los agentes personalizados automatizan el trabajo repetitivo de todo el equipo. Basta con definir un disparador o una programación y el agente se encarga del resto, las 24 horas del día, estés online o no. Lo crea una persona y lo aprovecha todo el equipo. [Más información.](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/custom-agent)

¿Cómo utiliza la IA de Notion mis datos?

Seguimos nuestras [prácticas estándar de protección de datos](https://www.notion.com/security)
 para mantener tu información cifrada y privada. La IA de Notion no utilizará tus datos para entrenar nuestros modelos, a menos que aceptes explícitamente compartirlos.

Cualquier información utilizada para impulsar la IA de Notion se comparte con subprocesadores de IA exclusivamente para ofrecerte las funciones de la IA de Notion. Contamos con acuerdos contractuales específicos con estos subprocesadores que prohíben el uso de los datos de los clientes para entrenar sus modelos. [Puedes ver más información sobre nuestras prácticas de seguridad y privacidad de la IA de Notion aquí.](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-ai-security-practices)

¿Cuánto cuesta la IA de Notion? (¿Y qué son los créditos de Notion?)

La IA de Notion está incluida en los planes Business y Enterprise de Notion, con funciones básicas como el agente de Notion, el Anotador con IA y la Búsqueda Enterprise. Los espacios de trabajo de otros planes tienen un uso de prueba limitado para conocer cómo funciona.

**¿Por qué los agentes personalizados tienen un precio diferente?**

Los agentes personalizados pueden ejecutarse con una frecuencia determinada o con disparadores, y llevar a cabo tareas de varios pasos en tu espacio de trabajo y las herramientas conectadas. Los administradores pueden adquirir créditos de Notion como complemento en los planes Business y Enterprise. Los créditos de Notion permiten a los equipos aumentar o reducir el uso según la cantidad de automatizaciones que ejecuten. [Más información](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/custom-agent-pricing)
.

**¿Qué son los créditos de Notion?**

Los agentes personalizados funcionan con créditos de Notion. Estos créditos están disponibles como complemento en los planes Business y Enterprise para los equipos que necesitan tener determinadas automatizaciones siempre activas. Cada ejecución consume créditos en función de la cantidad de trabajo que realice el agente, y los administradores pueden monitorizar el uso en el panel de control de los créditos de Notion. [Más información](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/notion-credits-dashboard)
.

**¿Cuándo entran en vigor los créditos de Notion?**

**Desde ahora hasta el 3 de mayo de 2026:**

Los agentes personalizados se pueden usar gratis en los planes Business y Enterprise, incluidos los periodos de prueba de Business. Durante este tiempo, los equipos pueden utilizarlos para descubrir cómo encajan en sus flujos de trabajo, y los administradores pueden monitorizar los patrones de su equipo en el [panel de control de los créditos de Notion](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/notion-credits-dashboard)
 para entender los patrones de uso y estimar cuántos créditos necesitarán en un futuro.

Los administradores (planes Business y Enterprise) pueden gestionar quién puede crear agentes personalizados y desactivar estos en cualquier momento para controlar su implementación.

**A partir del 4 de mayo de 2026:**

Los agentes personalizados empezarán a utilizar créditos de Notion cada vez que se ejecuten. Los administradores pueden comprar créditos adicionales y, si en algún momento no hay suficientes, los agentes se detendrán automáticamente hasta que se añadan más.

¿Cómo puedo saber más sobre la IA de Notion?

Visita nuestro [Centro de ayuda](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/notion-ai-faqs)
 y [Notion Academy](https://academy.notion.com/)
 : allí encontrarás guías, ejemplos y las mejores prácticas para usar la IA de Notion y los agentes personalizados.

How to apply
------------

[Apply now →](https://notion.pages.dev.notion.co/380b35e6e67f80849158f9152621c056)

![laptop-people](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F2IbsF6gv8I4kzUBMXFjhMj%2F1b13aff237a2cdbcb859cd32e35fb886%2Flaptop-people.png&w=1920&q=75)

### Apply

Notion verifies organizations in-house using the documents you provide us and public databases. Please submit all of your documentation along with your application to ensure our team can verify your organization.

![Acme Inc company wiki](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F5WvKyycMSevMgRZQdpnDBw%2F37b6be18644d8606bec9d970b1896ddc%2FAirplane_Case_Study_Illustration.png&w=1080&q=75)

### Process

Your organization must currently be on the Plus Plan in order to receive the 50% discount. If you are on a Free Plan, please upgrade to Plus when you apply for the discount. Once your organization is verified, our team will automatically apply the discount and you will receive an automatic email from Notion notifying you of this change.

![Acme Inc company wiki](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F7nhSBMG8f49XYhOPWOi0V9%2F6d7247bf5ac4e14a1bd764053af74b46%2Fpen.webp&w=1080&q=75)

### Upgrade

Currently, this program is only eligible for the Plus Plan. We are actively working on expanding the nonprofit discount to our Business plan.

![Acme Inc company wiki](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F6Is3zXg1bwF1Yla7U6rcHE%2Fa8d685e4e0abf6b7675cb41b21e025b1%2Fboxes.png&w=1080&q=75)

-------------------------------

Get started running your team in Notion with these pre-made setups. Click Duplicate at the top right to add to your workspace.

### Nonprofit fundraising

Use this template to keep track of individual donations and foundation/corporate fundraising with your team.

[Duplicate template→](https://www.notion.so/notion/Nonprofit-Fundraising-8f7d01b7f11c4787a532ed65fd6eba2f)

### Board management

Consider this a home for everything about your board—from contact info to meeting notes.

Questions & answers
-------------------

How do I apply for the Notion for Nonprofits discount?

To apply, please submit your organization’s information via the [Notion form](https://notion.pages.dev.notion.co/380b35e6e67f80849158f9152621c056)
. Once your organization is verified, our team will automatically apply the discount to your Plus Plan. If you are on a Free Plan, please upgrade to Plus when you apply for the discount. Once your nonprofit status is verified, our team will automatically apply the discount and notify you via email. After receiving this confirmation, please contact [\[email protected\]](https://www.notion.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#5a3435342a28353c332e291a373b313f34352e33353474393537)
 to request a refund for any eligible Plus Plan purchase made before the discount was applied.

To submit your application, Notion needs your Workspace ID. You can find this ID under Settings → General, at the very bottom of the tab.

If you have any question about the discount process, please reach out to [\[email protected\]](https://www.notion.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#6111130e030e0f0e210c000a040f0e15080e0f4f020e0c)
.

Each organization can request discounts for up to three workspaces.

What happens after I submit my application?

After you submit your application through the [Notion form](https://notion.pages.dev.notion.co/380b35e6e67f80849158f9152621c056)
, the Notion team will verify your application in 3–7 business days.

I submitted an application for the Notion for Nonprofits discount program. When should I hear back?

Thanks for applying! You'll hear back from us in 3-5 business days.

I am an educator/staff at a K-12 institution. Can I apply?

We offer 50% off our Plus plans for administrators, staff, and educators in K-12. We require documentation supporting your institution’s accreditation and/or nonprofit status in the application form. Reach out to your institution’s central administrator for the documentation.

I am an educator/staff at a higher education institution. Can I apply?

Yes. We offer 50% off our Plus plans for administrators, staff, and educators. We require documentation supporting your institution’s accreditation status in the application form. Reach out to your institution’s central administrator for the documentation.

I am part of a nonprofit student club / organization. Can I apply?

Yes! We require documentation supporting your organization’s nonprofit accreditation status in the application form.

Still have more questions? [Message support](https://www.notion.com/help)

We’re in this together

Questions & answers
-------------------

Which email provider(s) are Notion Mail compatible with?

Notion Mail integrates with Google and Gmail accounts.

When will Notion Mail be available on mobile devices?

Notion Mail is [available now on iOS](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/notion-mail/id6504265936)
 with Android coming very soon!

What languages are Notion Mail available in?

Notion Mail is currently available in English. We will support an additional thirteen languages (just like Notion!) very soon.

Can I manage multiple emails accounts on Notion Mail?

Yes! You can use multiple Notion accounts to manage different emails. We currently do not offer a unified inbox that shows emails from all your accounts in one place.

What are Notion Mail’s security standards?

Notion Mail is SOC2-certified and HIPAA-compliant, just like Notion. It also respects the same terms and privacy policies you already trust. [Learn more.](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-mail-security-practices)

### No training on your data

We have contractual agreements with our AI subprocessors that prohibit the use of customer data to train their models.

### SOC 2 Type 2 & ISO 27001

Notion is committed to the highest requirements of information security.

### GDPR & CCPA

We have mapped our privacy program to the GDPR and other global privacy regulations.

### Secure encryption

When you use Notion AI, your data is encrypted in-transit using TLS 1.2 or greater.

### Zero data retention for Enterprise

No data is stored with LLM providers. 30 day retention for non-Enterprise.

[Contact sales→](https://www.notion.com/contact-sales)

### HIPAA compliant for Enterprise

Notion AI enables HIPAA compliance by utilizing LLM provider’s zero-retention APIs and allows for the processing of protected health information (PHI).

[Contact sales→](https://www.notion.com/contact-sales)

See what Notion AI can do.

Questions & answers
-------------------

What can Notion AI help me do?

Notion AI is your built-in teammate inside Notion, working directly in your pages, docs, tasks, and databases so you can move faster without switching tools. Using context from your workspace and connected apps (when enabled), it helps you turn ideas into finished work all in one place.

**Here’s what you can do with Notion AI:**

*   Chat with [**Notion Agent**](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-ai-faqs#personal-agent)
     to take on entire tasks, using context from your workspace and connected apps to create and edit pages and databases.
    
*   Use [**Custom Agents**](https://www.notion.com/help/custom-agent)
     to automate recurring work for your team, like answering questions on Slack, routing tasks, and sharing project updates .
    
*   Search across your workspace and connected apps like Slack and Google Drive with [**Enterprise Search**](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-ai-faqs#enterprise-search)
     and [**Notion AI Connectors**](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-ai-connectors)
    ,, so you can find answers without jumping between tools.
    
*   Capture meetings with [**AI Meeting Notes**](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-ai-faqs#ai-meeting-notes-(beta))
    , which transcribe conversations, summarize key points, and surface insights automatically.
    
*   Dive deep on a topic with [**Research Mode**](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-ai-faqs#research-mode)
     to generate detailed reports and summaries.
    
*   Improve writing or generate drafts with [**AI blocks**](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-ai-faqs#notion-ai-inline)
     directly in your pages.
    
*   Create [**databases**](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-ai-faqs#notion-ai-for-databases)
    , auto-populate properties with [**Autofill**](https://www.notion.com/help/autofill#autofill)
    , and write formulas for smarter workflows and automations.
    

To ensure optimal performance and fair use across all Notion AI users, your access to AI features can be temporarily reduced depending on your usage.

What are Custom Agents?

Custom Agents automate recurring work for your entire team. Set a trigger or schedule, and the agent handles it from there—24/7, whether you're online or not. One person builds it, and the whole team benefits. [Learn more.](https://www.notion.com/help/custom-agent)

How does Notion AI use my data?

We follow our standard [data protection practices](https://www.notion.com/security)
 to keep your data encrypted and private. Notion AI will not use your data to train our models unless you opt in to a request to share your data.

Any information used to power Notion AI will be shared with AI subprocessors for the sole purpose of providing you with the Notion AI features. We specifically have contractual agreements in place with our AI subprocessors that prohibit the use of customer data to train their models. [Learn more about Notion AI security and privacy practices here.](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-ai-security-practices)

How much does Notion AI cost? (and what are Notion credits)?

Notion AI is included with Notion’s Business and Enterprise plans, with core features like Notion Agent, AI Meeting Notes, and Enterprise Search. Workspaces on other plans get a limited amount of trial usage to try it out.

**Why are Custom Agents priced differently?**

Custom Agents can run on schedules or triggers and complete multi-step work across your workspace and connected tools. Admins can purchase Notion credits as an add-on for Business and Enterprise plans. Notion credits let teams scale that usage up or down based on how much automation they run. [Learn more](https://www.notion.com/help/custom-agent-pricing)
.

**What are Notion credits?**

Custom Agents run on Notion credits. Notion credits are available as an add-on to Business and Enterprise plans for teams that need always-on automation. Each run uses credits based on how much work the agent does, and admins can track usage in the Notion credits dashboard. [Learn more](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-credits-dashboard)
.

**When do Notion credits go into effect?**

**Now through May 3, 2026:**

Custom Agents are free to use on Business and Enterprise plans, including Business trials. During this time, teams can explore how Custom Agents fit into their workflows, and admins can track their team's patterns in the [Notion credits dashboard](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-credits-dashboard)
 to understand usage and estimate future credit needs.

Admins (Business and Enterprise plans) can manage who can create Custom Agents and disable Agents anytime to guide controlled rollouts.

**Starting May 4, 2026:**

Custom Agents will start using Notion credits when they run. Admins can purchase additional credits, and if credits are insufficient, agents will automatically pause until more are added.

How can I learn more about Notion AI?

Visit our [Help Center](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-ai-faqs)
 and [Notion Academy](https://academy.notion.com/)
 for guides, examples, and best practices for using Notion AI and Custom Agents.

---

# Enterprise Search security & privacy practices – Notion Help Center

* * *

Notion's Enterprise Search enables your workspace to securely search and analyze content from connected applications (like Slack, Microsoft Teams, Jira, and more) via [Notion AI Connectors](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-ai-connectors)
. This document provides comprehensive security and privacy information for teams evaluating Notion's Enterprise Search capabilities.

Enterprise Search and AI Connectors follow [Notion’s AI Security & Privacy practices](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-ai-security-practices)
.

[Architecture overview](https://www.notion.com/help/enterprise-search-security-and-privacy-practices#architecture-overview)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Notion AI Connectors use a secure, privacy-preserving architecture to index and search your connected data.

Notion receives an embedding for data coming in through connected apps with AI Connectors and stores it in a vector database (e.g., Turbopuffer). The vector database is a data store optimized for embeddings that enables fast lookup of the most relevant pages given a user request.

![hc: enterprise search architecture overview](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2FpjSfUdZf4Xc91YpL3qh0s%2F1c3f4fc7be59672c0df13466c7b9fa43%2FAI_Connector_Architecture_from_Enterprise_Search_Security___Privacy_Practices.png&w=3840&q=75)

### **Key architecture components**

**Secure API connections**

*   OAuth 2.0 authentication with Microsoft, Atlassian, and Slack
    
*   All connections use TLS 1.2 or greater encryption in transit
    
*   Zero-retention API calls to prevent data storage at the connector level
    

**Embedding**

*   Content is processed into embeddings (numerical representations) that preserve meaning while protecting privacy
    
*   Uses OpenAI's zero-retention embeddings API
    
*   For details on how embeddings work, see [this article](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-ai-security-practices#embeddings)
    

**Vector database**

*   Embeddings stored in Turbopuffer, a SOC 2 Type 2 certified vector database
    
*   Enables fast, semantic search while maintaining security
    
*   Complete data isolation between customer workspaces
    

**Query process**

*   All queries respect user permissions for each connected app (permissions sync periodically; see [individual AI Connector documentation](https://www.notion.com/help/category/notion-ai)
     for specific details)
    
*   Results filtered based on user's access rights in both Notion and connected apps
    
*   No caching of sensitive content
    

### Security principles

**Data encryption**

*   Encryption keys managed by Notion's key management infrastructure
    
*   Embeddings in vector databases are encrypted at rest
    

**In transit**

*   When you use Notion AI, your data is encrypted in-transit using TLS 1.2 or greater
    
*   End-to-end encryption between Notion and all sub-processors
    

### Permission synchronization

*   Permissions checked at query time, not just during indexing
    
*   User mapping between Notion and connected services verified continuously
    
*   Changes in source system permissions reflected within 1 hour (can take longer for large workspaces)
    
*   Deleted content will become unsearchable; this can take around 30 minutes to one hour. See [individual AI Connector documentation](https://www.notion.com/help/category/notion-ai)
     for specific details.
    

[Data protection and privacy](https://www.notion.com/help/enterprise-search-security-and-privacy-practices#data-protection-and-privacy)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Data retention and deletion

**Automatic deletion timelines**

*   When you disconnect a connector: Data deleted within 24 hours
    
*   When source data is deleted: Immediately unsearchable, embeddings deleted within 60 days
    
*   When a Notion workspace is deleted: All associated embeddings deleted within 60 days
    
*   LLM providers retain data for 0 days (Enterprise) or a maximum of 30 days (all other plans)
    

**Customer control**

*   Request immediate deletion through `Settings` → `Notion AI` → `{connected app}` → `Disconnect`
    
*   Deletion requests processed automatically without manual intervention
    
*   Audit trail available for deletion confirmations
    

### GDPR and privacy rights

**Data subject rights reported**

*   Right to deletion: Remove specific content or entire connector data
    
*   Right to portability: Export embeddings and metadata
    
*   Data Processing Addendum (DPA) available for all customers
    

### Data synchronization security

**During the initial 36-hour sync period**

*   All data transfers use encrypted channels (TLS 1.2+)
    
*   Incremental processing prevents system overload
    
*   No temporary copies stored in unsecured locations
    
*   Rate limiting prevents abuse and ensures stable connections
    
*   Failed syncs automatically retry with exponential backoff
    
*   Progress monitoring available in connector settings
    

**Security measures during sync**

*   Continuous permission validation throughout sync process
    
*   Anomaly detection for unusual data volumes
    
*   Automatic pause if authentication errors detected
    
*   No data accessible via search until sync completes successfully
    
*   Audit trail of all sync activities and errors
    

[Access controls and permissions](https://www.notion.com/help/enterprise-search-security-and-privacy-practices#access-controls-and-permissions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Identity management

**Authentication requirements**

*   Workspace owners required for initial connector setup
    
*   Admin privileges needed in source systems (Slack admin, Google Workspace admin, etc.)
    
*   Our connectors automatically link users who have the same primary email in Notion and in the connected app. Users who do not use the same primary email in the connected app will see a prompt asking them to auth.
    
*   Guest users explicitly excluded from AI Connector access
    

See [individual AI Connector documentation](https://www.notion.com/help/category/notion-ai)
 for specific details.

[Third-party security and sub-processors](https://www.notion.com/help/enterprise-search-security-and-privacy-practices#third-party-security-and-sub-processors)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Current sub-processors

Notion is model agnostic; we will continue to evaluate and incorporate the latest and greatest AI models. For features like Research Mode, we will use a variety of different models to perform multiple searches in order to provide the most comprehensive responses.

*   **OpenAI**: Embeddings generation (zero retention)
    
*   **Anthropic**: LLM queries (zero retention for Enterprise)
    
*   **Turbopuffer**: Vector database (SOC 2 Type 2 certified)
    

### Models are not trained on your data

*   Notion has contractual agreements with all AI providers that prohibit training on customer data
    
*   Notion uses various large language models (LLMs) with zero-retention processing
    
*   Embeddings cannot be reverse-engineered to recover original content
    
*   No customer data is used to improve Notion's or any third-party's models
    

[Compliance and certifications](https://www.notion.com/help/enterprise-search-security-and-privacy-practices#compliance-and-certifications)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Notion's certifications

**Current compliance**

*   SOC 2 Type 2 (annually renewed)
    
*   ISO 27001:2022 certified
    
*   HIPAA compliant (with BAA for Enterprise)
    
*   GDPR compliant with appointed DPO
    
*   CCPA compliant
    

**AI Connector coverage**

*   Included in SOC 2 Type 2 scope
    
*   Covered under ISO 27001 certification
    
*   HIPAA compliance enabled through zero-retention APIs
    

### Industry standards

**Security frameworks**

*   NIST Cybersecurity Framework aligned
    
*   OWASP Top 10 protections
    
*   CIS Controls implementation
    
*   Regular third-party penetration testing
    

[Incident response](https://www.notion.com/help/enterprise-search-security-and-privacy-practices#incident-response)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Response process

**Our commitment**

*   24/7 security incident response team
    
*   Defined escalation procedures
    
*   72-hour breach notification (or faster per local requirements)
    
*   Root cause analysis for all security events
    
*   Transparent communication through [status.notion.com](http://status.notion.com/)
    

### Customer notification

**What we'll tell you**

*   Nature and scope of any incident
    
*   Affected data and systems
    
*   Remediation steps taken
    
*   Recommendations for customer action
    
*   Ongoing updates until resolution

Questions & Answers
-------------------

How does Notion AI search across multiple apps?

Using AI connectors, Notion AI performs internal knowledge search by indexing content from your work tools based on your permissions. When you ask a question, it searches Slack messages, files and PDFs in Google Drive, Jira tickets, GitHub Issues & Pull Requests, and other connected apps to deliver the most relevant information—fast.

Which tools can I connect to Notion AI?

You can connect apps like Slack, Google Drive, GitHub, Jira, MSFT Teams, SharePoint, OneDrive today with others coming soon: Linear, Gmail, Salesforce, Zendesk, Box and more. These connections enable a true unified search experience across all your internal and external knowledge sources.

Is Notion AI secure?

Yes. Notion AI only shows information you have permission to access. It follows strict security standards like SOC 2 Type 2, ISO 27001, GDPR, and CCPA compliance, with zero data retention for enterprise users. Read more about our [enterprise search security and privacy practices](https://www.notion.com/help/enterprise-search-security-and-privacy-practices.)

Can Notion AI create reports from multiple sources?

Absolutely. With Research Mode, Notion AI analyzes data from your connected apps and the web to generate detailed, ready-to-share reports—saving teams days of manual research.

Can I choose which sources Notion AI searches?

Yes. You control where and how Notion AI searches by selecting which apps, documents, and web sources to include—giving you full control over your search experience.

How is Notion AI different from traditional enterprise search tools?

Unlike traditional search, Notion AI doesn't just find files—it understands questions, retrieves up-to-date answers with citations, and even uses critical thinking to analyze complex questions and generate detailed research reports in minutes.

![](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F5qhbS8W459wXYXjysg9cqO%2F0052596ef70fc824a4defad24a16eee3%2Fnotion_qa_3.png&w=2048&q=75)

> What used to take hours of debugging can now be solved in minutes just by asking Notion AI.

![](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F6bBPA43NVmVSkFzvzxgAhE%2F543c517f4626cd68e285bd7eeacf62fd%2FOpenAI_Logo.png&w=1080&q=75)

John Allard

Engineering, OpenAI

What's included in Business and Enterprise plans?

Both plans include unlimited AI features, private team spaces, advanced database capabilities, and enhanced security controls. Enterprise adds organization-wide admin features, dedicated support, and custom security settings.

How do I know if my team needs to upgrade?

Consider upgrading if you need:

*   More powerful AI tools and enterprise search
    
*   Private spaces for sensitive work
    
*   Advanced database features
    
*   Enhanced security controls
    

Learn more about specific features in our [detailed pricing guide](https://www.notion.com/1cfb35e6e67f80a2a77ed98772d1a3b2)
.

What happens to my existing workspace when I upgrade?

Your workspace content and settings remain intact when you upgrade. You'll immediately gain access to new features while keeping all your existing work and configurations.

What is Notion AI?

Notion AI is our built-in artificial intelligence tool that helps teams work smarter. It includes features like Enterprise Search across all your work apps, automated meeting notes, research assistance, writing help, and translation capabilities - all integrated seamlessly into your Notion workspace. It's designed to help teams find information faster, automate routine tasks, and collaborate more effectively.

How do I get in touch with the Notion team?

You can reach our sales team by filling out the form above and we'll get back to you shortly. For immediate assistance, you can also schedule a demo where we can discuss your team's specific needs and show you how Notion AI can work for your organization.

# Join the Technology Partner Program | Notion

How to become a Notion technology partner
-----------------------------------------

Notion works best when it's connected with the other tools that power your work. Notion technology partners help build those integrations — connecting workflows, driving productivity, and delighting our joint users.

![Sapling](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F7ib3dWcEY1n9AEiQZoIfTS%2F282343ab2ff33358b1dc955d575a2718%2Ftools.png&w=1080&q=75)

### Build a Notion integration

Develop a public Notion integration that extends the value of our products (1+1=3).

### Get in touch

Submit the form on this page to tell us about your integration and connect with our team.

### Grow with us

We work with select technology partners to develop a joint story and distribute their integration.

![Typeform](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F1Umb6xlu1wfly4nTBSC1k1%2Fcda1bb8247b0fd868c62450b3e198b18%2Fslack-logo.png&w=640&q=75)![Cron](https://images.ctfassets.net/spoqsaf9291f/502ApiNcRHgIwrDU8XRYTQ/497492503acb3fa21bbd9dd1aec193c3/Figma-logo-color.svg)![Cron](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2FiwV1V6XLuOhKSYjyQaEIG%2F5bbf12a4069be570481cafc7ece62390%2Flogo_github.png&w=1920&q=75)![Cron](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F3YRJbO3SPLn2WN4A9hbDWA%2F49101e43b54926712d394f204f5364dc%2Flogo_zoom.png&w=1920&q=75)![Cron](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F2nQSBAKP1EbkLsnE35AI4H%2F1108e8b62f1944c8e9c2439e2f5e9083%2Floom_logo_lockup_color.png&w=640&q=75)![Cron](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F61QB4ecjMehci9Bmz6Vz4B%2F92bd7a16ac588f3e461988a752554bde%2Flogo_zapier.png&w=1920&q=75)![Typeform](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F5Q6J4GyljVbRIpjIEUWqpN%2Fa60738afaafd23eb23c493e8bc58db7f%2Flogo_dropbox.png&w=1920&q=75)![Cron](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F7sz4trMSQbO2JufUutkJnU%2Fa6bebb6cacc87ea32a5c8243dd8d6cd7%2Flogo_gitlab.png&w=1920&q=75)![Cron](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F76KVPU7tcAl3wzI2qjtrSr%2Fcf73e3909c42a91084dd08e144b56cf4%2Flogo_googledrive.png&w=1920&q=75)![Cron](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F3TMfZQ9Sx2ZRW7kWAS9nDa%2Fcc89ba33f488f72d468764f16ef5c71d%2Ftypeform.png&w=640&q=75)![Cron](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F6dAUjMIl88freVWUO4Vz3F%2Fc83e9c6edb723ee4e674a1dce617d931%2Flogo_jira.png&w=1920&q=75)![Cron](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F1zE6K2hY4uOItUrnQDPrvs%2F0bcb9684c25e2fd6d982656c97e90a3a%2Flogo_make.png&w=1920&q=75)

> Figma’s integrations with Notion offer a seamless and visual way to use our tools in concert, delighting our joint users and making work more collaborative.

![Notion logo](https://images.ctfassets.net/spoqsaf9291f/502ApiNcRHgIwrDU8XRYTQ/497492503acb3fa21bbd9dd1aec193c3/Figma-logo-color.svg)

**Anna Kohnen**Head of Partnerships, Figma

Questions & answers
-------------------

I have built a Notion integration — do I qualify to become a Notion technology partner?

Having a live public integration is a key prerequisite to becoming a Notion technology partner. We are looking for partners that thoughtfully extend Notion’s capabilities with integrations that our customers use and love. But integrations alone don't make a partnership — we want to work with partners who share our focus, mission, and vision. If you believe your integration and company are a fit, please fill out the form linked on this page and our partnership team will reach out!

I submitted my interest in becoming a technology partner; when can I expect to hear back?

We're not accepting new applications to the Technology partner program right now. If you'd like, you can still share more about your company and integration in the form above, and we'll reach out as soon as the program reopens.

I haven't built an integration with Notion yet. Where do I start?

The Notion API is publicly available for anyone to explore. You can find our documentation and get started at [developers.notion.com](https://developers.notion.com/)
. You can create internal integrations for private use or build public integrations that are available to Notion users and apply to become a Notion technology partner afterward.

I’m interested in becoming a security and compliance partner. Where do I learn more?

Please apply to our Technology Partner Program using the form on this webpage and note that you’re an interested security and compliance partner. You can find high-level information about the program here; and we’ll be in touch with additional information once we’ve had a chance to review your application.

Still have more questions?

[Message support](https://www.notion.com/contact)

Infinitely configurable, so you can work the way you want
---------------------------------------------------------

### Capture every detail in a database

Track all your important information in one place, so nothing slips through the cracks. Combine multiple data sources and prevent information silos.

![Launch checklist](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F5kXRXwCLL3fQ3hpRcxPB90%2Fd2b0da73dfc81ff9a5748b07a63dc680%2Fdatabase-container.png&w=3840&q=75)

### View projects as a timeline for a bird's eye view

See the bigger picture of how projects fit together, so you can resolve dependencies and hit your deadlines.

![Product roadmap](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F4P5q1wv9rzcLEtnZljyXZq%2F24b70da8c1cffe0819f055f4ff0b9a49%2Fproject-roadmap.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Visualize progress with charts

Create a dashboard with charts from as many sources as you want.

![Project tracker](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F3DAED7C6wAc8RlCM1nJyE5%2F6483648c84c7dbb748cc9707507c4b17%2Fproject-tracker.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Choose the exact info you want to track

Create your own priority labels, status tags, and more, so every team can craft the perfect workflow.

![Feature database properties](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F1nwID3ru5rwMMO4uzNv8va%2F247643254024b08fc62a7edf577b1440%2Ffeature-database-properties-V3.png&w=2048&q=75)

### Automate your team workflows

Spend less time on manual tasks with automations that streamline task flows, bug reports, database entries, doc outlines and more.

![Workflow automation](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F5zOaIyfOaEleo9mjrkKhWG%2F21e313a10dbc19dd82e294052b33173d%2Fhigh-perf-teams-V3.png&w=2048&q=75)

### Filter and sort info to see what you need

Show only tasks assigned to you, or items marked as urgent. Break down any complex project in the way that’s most helpful to you.

![Filtered kanban view](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F6rIlyH477Pd7UHscCYMz2s%2F5fa0c3b7809ab984e085b4cf01965a7b%2Ffeature-filter-kanban.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Capture requests with forms

Collect information from your team. Then kick off tasks and workflows.

![Form](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F6IoRho5AkfqFdIQTQMCr8B%2Fbee13749f3f9e6d309c52066f83901ac%2Ffeature-forms.png&w=1920&q=75)

### Customize the layout of your tasks and projects

Create a unique design that fits how you and your team work.

![Layout](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F4Y43iiZ4wPKlH7JBPHmo7c%2F25e6b350a095f9e63a0dc5e45bd8fb50%2Ffeature-layouts.png&w=2048&q=75)

### Control who can see and edit

Set granular permissions in your databases without manual sharing. Page-level access rules automatically grant permissions based on assignee or owner, ensuring team members only access what’s relevant to them.

![Acme Inc company wiki](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2FEQLeWOrJ9GVjqGiDGNwYi%2F645d3fa351133cf69b6a8c4a3811dd1c%2Fpermissions.png&w=3840&q=75)

Catch all the details, big and small
------------------------------------

### Tasks and sub-tasks

Break projects into manageable pieces to get the work done.

### Status, assignee, due date

So everyone knows what to do and when to do it.

### Database views

Visualize the work in distinct formats, from calendars to boards.

### Dependencies

See when one task is blocking another and avoid bottlenecks.

### My tasks

Manage every task assigned to you in one place.

### Progress bar

See how your project is tracking toward its launch.

Focus on what's important. Leave the rest to AI.

# Notion Security & Compliance | SOC 2 Certified, trusted by Enterprises

Security
--------

Notion takes a security-by-design approach to protecting your data. Our team continues to make investments so you can use Notion with confidence.

[Our security practices →](https://www.notion.com/help/security-and-privacy)

![Spot Illustration: Lock key holes - Blue](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F7dU3O8gnlsIkhli1vq4p7D%2Fd4b38bed30a4992f9e6139c7d394eb8c%2FLock_key_holes.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Security infrastructure

Notion’s infrastructure is designed with layers of protection to help ensure your data is secure while transmitted, stored, or processed. Protections include but are not limited to encryption, least privilege access, secure software development, and a public bug bounty program.

[Submit Vulnerability Report→](https://hackerone.com/b21888db-e0d1-48cd-b61b-55aaa96600d4/embedded_submissions/new)

### Operational security

Our information security team continuously implements new security controls and monitors Notion for malicious activity across our infrastructure, networks, and assets.

### Product security

Notion provides a robust set of in product data protection and admin controls for greater visibility and control over our data. Enterprise admins can deploy Notion to their organizations with SSO via SAML 2.0, provision users through SCIM, and track activity with the audit log features. Enterprise admins can also fine tune permission controls and guests, and manage team organizations.

Privacy
-------

Notion maintains a comprehensive privacy compliance program and is committed to partnering with its customers and vendors on privacy compliance efforts.

![Spot Illustration: Dog at fence - blue](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F2YwomD27oPDl5M4Xkve6CD%2F7b356526cbd9e8cb2e0b16a3533bb071%2FDog_at_fence.png&w=1920&q=75)

### How we handle your data

At Notion our team is dedicated to developing and implementing data privacy processes and safeguards that meet industry standards and best practices. We conduct ongoing training for our teams to ensure that they are up to speed with developments in legislation and essential privacy and security practices. Every Notion employee and contractor signs up to non-disclosure terms to maintain the confidentiality and security of your data. Notion also holds any vendors that handle personal data to the same data management, security, and privacy practices and standards to which we hold ourselves.

### Agreements

At Notion we strive to keep all of our agreements up to date with the latest regulations and industry standards. Our Master Subscription Agreement and Data Processing Addendum describe in detail Notion’s data privacy processes, standards, safeguards and our compliance with data protection legislation. To ensure that our terms track with the GDPR, CCPA and other global privacy standards we continually have our terms assessed by leading privacy experts in multiple jurisdictions.

### Data governance

Data governance relates to the policies and procedures that dictate how data is procured and used throughout its life cycle. From creation and collection to processing, distribution, storage and deletion. Notion’s commitment to data governance is key to keeping our users data secure, private, accurate, and accessible.

### GDPR

The General Data Protection Regulation (GDPR) is a comprehensive data protection law that governs the collection of and use of personal data of EU residents, and that allows data subjects to exercise control over their data. As the GDPR is widely considered to be the most stringent global privacy standard, we have mapped our privacy program to the GDPR and other global privacy regulations.

### Policies

At Notion we want to be as transparent as possible with our customers about how we collect, process, store, and use their personal data. In order to achieve this Notion maintains comprehensive and detailed policies regarding how we handle your personal information. These policies describe in detail how our users can exercise their rights with regard to their data.

[Our terms & privacy policy→](https://notion.notion.site/Terms-and-Privacy-28ffdd083dc3473e9c2da6ec011b58ac)

Compliance
----------

Notion maintains a comprehensive security and privacy program to provide advanced security features in our Enterprise plan that are designed to protect your data in accordance with various regulatory and industry standards. Notion has been attested by independent third-party auditors. If you’d like a copy of the compliance reports, please visit our Trust Center.

[Our Trust Center →](https://trust.notion.com/)

![Spot illustration: blueprints - blue ](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F6IOcGytvQ506uybKVbMxfH%2F350f6b83d12fb002a620db7d5fc66583%2Fpaper.png&w=3840&q=75)

### SOC 2 Type 2

The SOC 2 Type 2 is an audit report performed by an independent third-party certified by the American Institute of Certified Public Accountants (AICPA) to evaluate a service organization's controls related to the Trust Services Criteria (TSC). The SOC 2 Type 2 report assesses the effectiveness of these controls over a period of time and is intended to provide assurance to customers and stakeholders that the organization has implemented adequate controls to protect their data.

![Acme Inc company wiki](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F1FWv4AhXkSZRRKhXqrGE9a%2Fccda9dfe1fbb3acdbd3ac7b526fa8901%2Fsecurity-compliance-soc-2-type-2.png&w=1920&q=75)

### ISO 27001, ISO 27701, ISO 27017, ISO 27018

ISO is an international standard development organization, and Notion has achieved certifications for four ISO standards: ISO 27001, ISO 27701, ISO 27017, and ISO 27018. The standards outline requirements for establishing, implementing, and continuously improving Notion’s Information Security Management System (ISMS) and Privacy Information Management System (PIMS).

![Acme Inc company wiki](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F1PtvQNjLzIHOV1BdEsZwiJ%2F82e5046b08dbcf1610d4786d2d3ac2da%2Fsecurity-compliance-iso-v2.png&w=1920&q=75)

### HIPAA

The Health Insurance Portability and Accountability Act (HIPAA) is a US federal law that was enacted in 1996 that requires the protection and confidential handling of protected health information (PHI) by covered entities such as healthcare providers, health plans, and healthcare clearinghouses, as well as their business associates. Provided businesses subject to HIPAA leverage the Notion Enterprise-grade security features described in our Help Center article here and sign Notion’s Business Associate Agreement they may process PHI within their Notion workspace.

![Acme Inc company wiki](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F2quoFJCv2s9b91owAwVLDJ%2Fb0ff0f0f09b1ae6806338b19cadb15cc%2Fsecurity-compliance-hipaa.png&w=1920&q=75)

### BSI C5 (Cloud Computing Compliance Controls Catalogue)

BSI C5 is a security standard developed by the German Federal Office for Information Security. It outlines baseline security controls for cloud service providers. C5 includes additional control requirements relating to data location, service provisioning, place of jurisdiction, existing certifications, information disclosure obligations, and a full-service description.

![Acme Inc company wiki](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F3naUmSpP61tu3yD4IBUQAI%2F23f28dbd3ad3d56b244f06bd8ab8c5a9%2Fsecurity-compliance-bsi-c5.png&w=1920&q=75)

Artificial intelligence (AI) governance
---------------------------------------

Notion leverages AI to improve the core product experience and provide real value to our users in their day-to-day work. We strive to do this in a way that’s trustworthy, reliable, and user-centric.

![Spot Illustration: Rubik's cube - blue](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F658mqE8zbJjnsY8JSn5tLo%2F50f71d586babc9e69a12a27ad718b127%2FRubik-s_cube.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Safe & secure

Notion takes a safety-first approach to artificial intelligence. Our AI features and partners undergo security and legal reviews prior to Notion utilizing their services. These security practices apply to our AI features and AI development process.

[Our security practices→](https://www.notion.com/es-es/help/notion-ai-security-practices)

### Transparency

At Notion, we want to be transparent with our customers about our AI products. In order to achieve this Notion maintains a Help Center and Terms and Privacy page to outline how our AI products’ functionality and privacy practices.

[Our terms & privacy policy→](https://app.notion.com/p/notion/Terms-and-Privacy-28ffdd083dc3473e9c2da6ec011b58ac)

### Empowering

We aim to create AI-enhanced experiences that aren’t just interesting — but rather, genuinely useful in your day-to-day work. To achieve this, the development of our AI-powered features is grounded in extensive research to understand the needs of our users.

### Data governance

Your data is yours. Our AI Subprocessors are prohibited from using Customer Data to train models. The controls and permissions with respect to access and use of customer data will be respected.

Reliability
-----------

Notion is relied on from creatives to cooperations - as such, everyone deserves a platform they can count on. With robust uptime guarantees and multi-level redundancy, you can trust Notion will be there when you need it.

![Spot Illustration: Flexible tools pocket knife - Blue](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2FZmLtxhnUafKBGJyXJeK6Q%2F793cfb07fd456f1b293ac25e6e45c5d0%2Fflexible-tool.png&w=3840&q=75)

### High availability & Failover

Notion keeps your data safe by having multiple zones for redundancy, have a comprehensive backup program, and regularly testing our disaster recovery and business continuity program. Notion offers a guaranteed uptime of 99.9%, so users can trust that we’ll be there when you need us.

Ofertas de soporte proactivo y personalizado las 24 horas para equipos con necesidades más especializadas.

### Gestión de identidades

Integración SSO basada en SAML para un acceso seguro de los empleados.

### Aprovisionamiento de usuarios con SCIM

Crea, elimina, actualiza o recupera fácilmente cualquier usuario o grupo.

### Gestión del espacio de trabajo y del dominio

Herramientas centralizadas de seguridad, cumplimiento, estadísticas y auditoría.

### Normas de cumplimiento global

Certificaciones RGPD, HIPAA y CCPA.

### Certificaciones de seguridad de terceros

SOC 2 Tipo 2, BSI C5 e ISO (27001, 27701, 27017, 27018).

### Regulación de la IA

No hay entrenamiento ni almacenamiento de tus datos por parte de los proveedores de LLM.

### Protección de datos robusta

Cifrado AES-256 en reposo y TLS 1.2+ en tránsito.

### Residencia de datos

Opciones en centros de datos de la UE y EE. UU.

### Integraciones de socios de seguridad y cumplimiento

Integra con tus plataformas preferidas de SIEM, DLP y Cumplimiento.

FAQs
----

![](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=%2Ffront-static%2Fpages%2Ftemplates%2Fcategory-FAQ.png&w=256&q=75)

Does Notion support project templates for different industries?

Yes, Notion offers project templates for various industries, from software and marketing to construction and education. Each template can be customized to fit industry-specific workflows while maintaining core project management principles.

Do Notion project management tools allow custom workflow creation?

Yes. Notion's composable approach lets you create custom workflows tailored to your team's needs, combining different views and properties that can evolve as your projects change.

What does "composable project management" mean?

It's the idea of building your system from modular parts that can be reconfigured as needs change. Your project management tool, built by you, for you.

Is Notion good for project management?

Yes. Teams use Notion to manage plans, tasks, timelines, docs, and status updates in one place. Because templates are composable, you can tailor workflows (Agile, Waterfall, hybrid) without duct‑taping multiple tools together. Competitors offer templates too, but Notion's linked databases keep everything connected.

What project management templates should I start with?

Start with a project plan, timeline (Gantt), WBS, RACI, and a weekly status report. These together cover the four fundamentals of any project: scope, schedule, ownership, and communication.

Can I manage Agile projects in Notion?

Yes. Use a backlog and sprint board (Kanban), plus a timeline for capacity planning. Add retrospectives and a change log to complete the loop.

How do Notion templates compare to spreadsheets or docs?

Templates in spreadsheets are quick, but they're usually static. Notion templates create databases you can relate, filter, and visualize (board, timeline, calendar), with the flexibility to adapt as projects grow. Notion lets you bring docs, tasks, and wiki together in one space. No more SaaS sprawl!

---

Quien mucho cambia de herramienta, poco construye
-------------------------------------------------

![Ilustración: Caos (Rojo)](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F50o9qfDCrjQ1OsFD3V3JRn%2Fa0025ebb6e1a2114d2d8bd09dfdde846%2FMetaphoric-Spots_sprawl2_red-crop.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Equipos e información aislados

Tener la estrategia y la ejecución en herramientas separadas retrasa los lanzamientos.

### Falta de visibilidad

Los documentos, la información y las actualizaciones están dispersas… y se nota en la toma de decisiones.

### Pérdida de productividad

Horas perdidas en búsquedas, redacción y cambios de contexto, en vez de crear.

Lanza mejores productos, y más rápido, con un espacio de trabajo conectado
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Desarrollo de productos de principio a fin en un solo lugar

Analiza comentarios de clientes, redacta documentos de requisitos de producto (PRD), realiza un seguimiento del progreso y elabora planes de lanzamiento en un único espacio de trabajo conectado.

### Un lugar para todas tus herramientas

Integra tus aplicaciones clave y céntrate en lo importante. Menos interrupciones, más fluidez.

### Flujos de trabajo automatizados con IA

Optimiza las tareas manuales, como las notas de reunión, las acciones pendientes, los PRD y las actualizaciones de progreso. Céntrate en crear.

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sin fricciónLas entregas y los flujos de trabajo fluidos se traducen en lanzamientos más rápidos
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tus hojas de ruta, PRD y especificaciones técnicas siempre conectadas a proyectos y tareas. Con flujos de trabajo automatizados y actualizaciones, los equipos técnicos se mantienen alineados, sin pérdidas de información ni documentos desactualizados.

AdaptableFlexibilidad para crear el espacio de trabajo ideal para tu equipo
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

# System requirements for Notion – Notion Help Center

* * *

![](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=%2Ffront-static%2Fshared%2Fcallouts%2Ftip-illustration-v4.png&w=128&q=75)

For the best experience with Notion, make sure you’re using the latest version of your operating system or browser.

[Desktop](https://www.notion.com/help/system-requirements-for-notion#desktop)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Learn more about Notion for desktop here →](https://www.notion.so/help/notion-for-desktop)

| Operating system | Version |
| --- | --- |
| macOS | macOS 12 or above |
| Windows | Windows 10 version 21H2 or above<br><br>Windows Server 2016 |

[Web](https://www.notion.com/help/system-requirements-for-notion#web)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

[Learn more about Notion for web here →](https://www.notion.so/help/notion-for-web)

| Browser | Version |
| --- | --- |
| Chrome | The last eight major [Extended stable](https://support.google.com/chrome/a/answer/9027636)<br> releases |
| Firefox, Safari, Edge | The last two major releases |

[Mobile](https://www.notion.com/help/system-requirements-for-notion#mobile)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Learn more about Notion for mobile here →](https://www.notion.so/help/notion-for-mobile)

| Operating system | Version |
| --- | --- |
| iOS | iOS 17.0 or above |
| Android | Android 8 or above |

The following iOS devices aren't supported:

*   iPad Air 2
    
*   iPad Mini 4
    
*   iPad (5th generation) 2017
    
*   iPad Pro 9.7" 2016
    
*   iPad Pro 12.9" (1st generation) 2015
    
*   iPhone X 2017
    
*   iPhone 8 and 8 Plus 2017
    
*   iPhone 7
    
*   iPhone 6
    
*   iPhone 6s
    

* * *

* * *

[![](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F22rr0pA35XNmyGoq6HNz48%2F1de31582287cdbb7257efd80ff431736%2FNotion_for_mobile_beta_-_hero.png&w=3840&q=75)\
\
Up next\
\
Get early access to new mobile features before anyone else, and help shape the future of Notion’s iOS & Android apps! Compared to the standard mobile apps, you’ll receive bug fixes and updates much quicker 📲\
\
Read more→](https://www.notion.com/help/notion-for-mobile-beta-version "Notion beta program")

Flexibilidad infinita para que el trabajo se adapte a ti
--------------------------------------------------------

### Captura cada detalle en una base de datos

Controla toda tu información importante en un solo lugar, para que nada se pierda. Combina múltiples fuentes de datos y evita los silos de información.

![Lista de tareas para lanzamiento](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F5kXRXwCLL3fQ3hpRcxPB90%2Fd2b0da73dfc81ff9a5748b07a63dc680%2Fdatabase-container.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Visualiza los proyectos en forma de cronograma para tener una vista a largo plazo

Obtén una visión global de cómo encajan los proyectos, para resolver dependencias y cumplir con los plazos.

![Hoja de ruta del producto](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F4P5q1wv9rzcLEtnZljyXZq%2F24b70da8c1cffe0819f055f4ff0b9a49%2Fproject-roadmap.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Visualiza el progreso con gráficos

Crea un panel con gráficos a partir de todas las fuentes que quieras.

![Registro de proyectos](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F3DAED7C6wAc8RlCM1nJyE5%2F6483648c84c7dbb748cc9707507c4b17%2Fproject-tracker.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Elige la información que no quieres perder de vista

Crea tus propias etiquetas de prioridad, estados y mucho más, para que cada equipo pueda diseñar el flujo de trabajo perfecto.

![Propiedades destacadas de bases de datos](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F1nwID3ru5rwMMO4uzNv8va%2F247643254024b08fc62a7edf577b1440%2Ffeature-database-properties-V3.png&w=2048&q=75)

### Automatiza los flujos de trabajo de tu equipo

Dedica menos tiempo a tareas manuales con automatizaciones que agilizan flujos de trabajo, informes de errores, registros en bases de datos, esquemas de documentos y mucho más.

![Automatización de flujos de trabajo](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F5zOaIyfOaEleo9mjrkKhWG%2F21e313a10dbc19dd82e294052b33173d%2Fhigh-perf-teams-V3.png&w=2048&q=75)

### Filtra y ordena la información para ver justo lo que necesitas

Muestra solo las tareas que te han asignado o los elementos marcados como urgentes. Desglosa cualquier proyecto complejo de la forma que te resulte más útil.

![Vista Kanban filtrada](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F6rIlyH477Pd7UHscCYMz2s%2F5fa0c3b7809ab984e085b4cf01965a7b%2Ffeature-filter-kanban.png&w=3840&q=75)

### Captura solicitudes con formularios

Recopila información de tu equipo. A continuación, inicia las tareas y flujos de trabajo.

![Formulario](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F6IoRho5AkfqFdIQTQMCr8B%2Fbee13749f3f9e6d309c52066f83901ac%2Ffeature-forms.png&w=1920&q=75)

### Personaliza el diseño de tus tareas y proyectos

Crea un diseño único que se adapte a tu forma de trabajar y a la de tu equipo.

![Diseño](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2F4Y43iiZ4wPKlH7JBPHmo7c%2F25e6b350a095f9e63a0dc5e45bd8fb50%2Ffeature-layouts.png&w=2048&q=75)

### Controla quién puede ver y editar

Configura permisos granulares en tus bases de datos sin necesidad de compartir manualmente. Las reglas de acceso a nivel de página asignan permisos de forma automática según la persona responsable o propietaria, garantizando que cada miembro del equipo acceda solo a lo que le corresponde.

![Wiki de la empresa Acme S. A.](https://www.notion.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fspoqsaf9291f%2FEQLeWOrJ9GVjqGiDGNwYi%2F645d3fa351133cf69b6a8c4a3811dd1c%2Fpermissions.png&w=3840&q=75)

Que no se te escape ningún detalle
----------------------------------

### Tareas y subtareas

Convierte los proyectos en tareas alcanzables para terminarlos con éxito.

### Estado, responsable, fecha límite

Para que cada persona sepa qué hacer y en qué momento.

### Vistas de base de datos

Visualiza el trabajo en distintos formatos, desde calendarios hasta tableros.

### Dependencias

Anticípate a los bloqueos y evita cuellos de botella.

### Mis tareas

Gestiona todas las tareas que se te asignen en un solo lugar.

### Barra de progreso

Sigue de cerca el progreso de tu proyecto hasta el lanzamiento.

Enfócate en lo que importa, la IA se encarga del resto
------------------------------------------------------

### Redacta proyectos de más nivel y a mayor velocidad con la ayuda de la IA
